## DEC-P01-B1-001

- decision_id: `DEC-P01-B1-001`
- status: `RATIFIED`
- decision: Ratify `governance/PRODUCT_CHARTER.md` as the v1 Product Charter; document status `ratified_evolving`.
- ratified_by: `Rauf Alizada`
- ratified_at: `2026-06-20`
- source_task: `CONT-P01-BUNDLE-001`
- drafted_by: `Claude Code`
- reviewed_by: `Product Owner`
- evidence: commit `571a75115e20c8bcee61b338aa9ae69f2c355450` (Bundle 1 deliverable drafts) and the Bundle 1 ratification diff prepared under this task.
- scope_note: Ratifies the Product Charter only. Does not authorize Bundle 2–5 work (`GLOSSARY.md`, `CHANGE_PROTOCOL.md` updates, `NEVER_AUTOMATIC.md`, `TRUST_BOUNDARIES.md`, `RISK_REGISTER.md` top-six update, `docs/REFERENCE_STRUCTURE.md`, cold-start checklist ratification, roadmap update, adapter alignment, P01 closeout). Does not authorize architecture evaluation or selection, implementation work, implementation stack selection, license selection or creation, dependency installation, hook registration or activation, ADR creation, or modification of adapter rules (`CLAUDE.md`, `AGENTS.md`, `.claude/rules/`).

  - `P03-blocking` rows must be resolved, disposed, or explicitly deferred-with-acceptance under a separately approved Product Owner gate before P03 closeout.
  - `P04-blocking` rows need not be resolved for P03 closeout but must be resolved or explicitly accepted before P04 GO (source-package Gate G-8).
  - `deferred-with-acceptance` rows may remain open into P04 and possibly P05 with explicit Product Owner acceptance and require no scheduled resolution unless reclassified by a later Product Owner decision.
- reclassification: Any later change to a row's ratified classification requires a separately approved Product Owner diff that either supersedes this decision or amends it under a new decision id.
- evidence:
  - Proposed P03 G-4 Classification Planning Artifact committed at `e7654c2574644a9284e9f62cdc4e544b678c3c59` (`governance/P03_G4_CLASSIFICATION_PLAN.md`, `document_status: PROPOSED_INACTIVE`, `ratification_status: NOT_RATIFIED` before this decision).
  - This G-4 ratification diff.
- non_authorizations:
  - Does **not** mutate `governance/OPEN_QUESTIONS.md`.
  - Does **not** mutate `governance/RISK_REGISTER.md`.
  - Does **not** mutate `governance/ROADMAP.md`.
  - Does **not** resolve any `OQ-P02-*` row.
  - Does **not** accept, dispose, or otherwise transition any `P02-RISK-*` row.
  - Does **not** schedule any `P02-ROAD-*` roadmap item.
  - Does **not** ratify any architecture recommendation `R-1..R-6` from `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_EVALUATION_PACKAGE.md`.
  - Does **not** ratify any `ADR-DRAFT-P03-001..006` from `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_EVALUATION_PACKAGE.md`.
  - Does **not** modify `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_EVALUATION_PACKAGE.md`.
  - Does **not** modify `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_RATIFICATION_PLAN.md`.
  - Does **not** authorize implementation, project code, dependency installation, lockfile or manifest changes, license selection, hook registration or activation, settings changes (`.claude/settings.json`, `.claude/settings.local.example.json`), adapter-rule changes (`CLAUDE.md`, `AGENTS.md`, `.claude/rules/**`), runtime context pack generation (`.continuum/RUNTIME_CONTEXT.md`, `.continuum/context-index.yaml`, `.continuum/context-budget.yaml`, `.continuum/context-freshness.yaml`, `.continuum/token-audit.md`), or P04/P05 activation.
  - Does **not** create any P04 or P05 task.
  - Does **not** create or modify `governance/PRODUCT_OWNER.md` (absent and remains absent).
  - Does **not** project any P03-specific row into `governance/OPEN_QUESTIONS.md`, `governance/RISK_REGISTER.md`, or `governance/ROADMAP.md`.
- invariants_preserved:
  - Exactly one active task: `CONT-P03-ARCH-001` (active-task invariant preserved).
  - P04 and P05 remain not active; no P04 or P05 task is proposed or activated by this decision.
  - Ratified context-policy set remains canonical and is not superseded.

The identity `Tural Rahmanli` is not a project identity and must not be encoded as project authority; any incidental appearance of that name in Git committer metadata or environment metadata is not project authority.

## DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-001

Ratified criterion text: "Every ratified architecture recommendation carried forward from the P03 Architecture Evaluation Package must be recorded as a distinct `governance/DECISION_LOG.md` row." Each future per-recommendation ratification gate (`R-1..R-6`) must therefore produce exactly one distinct ratification row in `governance/DECISION_LOG.md`; merged-row ratifications across multiple recommendations are not permitted.

Every future ratified P03 architecture decision row in `governance/DECISION_LOG.md` (under the `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-NNN`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-NNN`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-NNN`, or `DEC-P03-ARCH-REVISION-NNN` families) must therefore include an explicit non-authorization / non-scope section enumerating what the decision does **not** authorize; ratification rows that omit a non-authorization / non-scope section are not permitted.

## DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-003

- decision_id: `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-003`
- status: `RATIFIED`
- decision: Ratify P03 implementation-readiness criterion `I-8` from `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_EVALUATION_PACKAGE.md` §8 as canonical procedural / phase-boundary discipline under `CONT-P03-ARCH-001`. Ratified criterion text: "P03 closeout requires a separately approved Product Owner P03 closeout decision, which flips `CONT-P03-ARCH-001` frontmatter to `lifecycle_status: DONE`, `gate_status: COMPLETED`, `ratification_status: RATIFIED`, `active: false`, `execution_authorized: false`, and records `closeout_decision`. P04 GO is a separately approved decision; closing P03 does not by itself activate P04." P03 closeout therefore requires a distinct Product Owner-approved closeout decision (anticipated under the `DEC-P03-CLOSEOUT-NNN` family); closing P03 does not by itself activate P04; and P04 activation requires its own separately approved Product Owner activation decision, single-active-task gate, and task creation.
- ratified_by: `Rauf Alizada`
- ratified_at: `2026-06-25`
- source_task: `CONT-P03-ARCH-001`
- source_activation: `DEC-P03-ACTIVATION-001`
- drafted_by: `Claude Code`
- reviewed_by: `Product Owner`
- criterion_ratified: `I-8` (`governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_EVALUATION_PACKAGE.md` §8).
- decision_family: `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-NNN` (per `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_RATIFICATION_PLAN.md` §9). This decision is the third row in the `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-NNN` family and is sequenced after `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-001` (which ratified `I-1`) and `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-002` (which ratified `I-7`).
- related_prior_decisions: `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-002`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001`, `DEC-P03-ACTIVATION-001`.
- safety_basis:
  - `I-8` is a procedural / phase-boundary discipline rule. It carries no direct content dependency on any unresolved `OQ-P02-*`, `P02-RISK-*`, or `P02-ROAD-*` row.
  - `I-8` does not require modifying `governance/OPEN_QUESTIONS.md`, `governance/RISK_REGISTER.md`, or `governance/ROADMAP.md`.
  - `I-8` does not require revising `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_EVALUATION_PACKAGE.md` or `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_RATIFICATION_PLAN.md`; both remain `PROPOSED_INACTIVE` / `NOT_RATIFIED` as canonical reference framing only.
  - `I-8` does not require modifying or reclassifying any row of `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001`.
  - `I-8` does not by itself ratify any recommendation, ADR, or other criterion; it only codifies the P03 closeout / P04 activation separation discipline that each future closeout or activation gate must satisfy.
  - `I-8` is complementary to `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-001` (`I-1` row-uniqueness rule) and `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-002` (`I-7` explicit-non-authorization disclosure rule) and does not conflict with either; the three procedural rules co-bind every future P03 ratification gate and every future phase-boundary gate.
- forward_application:
  - Closing P03 requires a distinct Product Owner-approved closeout decision recorded as a row in `governance/DECISION_LOG.md` under the `DEC-P03-CLOSEOUT-NNN` family (per `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_RATIFICATION_PLAN.md` §9). That closeout decision flips `governance/tasks/CONT-P03-ARCH-001.md` frontmatter to `lifecycle_status: DONE`, `gate_status: COMPLETED`, `ratification_status: RATIFIED`, `active: false`, `execution_authorized: false`, and records the `closeout_decision` reference; it does not by itself activate P04.
  - Activating P04 requires a separately approved Product Owner P04 activation decision (anticipated under a future `DEC-P04-ACTIVATION-NNN` family), a separately created P04 task that satisfies the single-active-task invariant, and a separately approved P04 GO gate. Closing P03 does not implicitly create or authorize a P04 task.
  - This forward-application clause restates and binds `I-8`; it does not authorize any P03 closeout, any P04 activation, or any P04 task.
- evidence:
  - `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_EVALUATION_PACKAGE.md` §8 carries `I-8` as a proposed implementation-readiness criterion (status: `proposed`; document remains `PROPOSED_INACTIVE` / `NOT_RATIFIED`).
  - `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_RATIFICATION_PLAN.md` §5 lists `I-8` among items ready for procedural ratification planning (document remains `PROPOSED_INACTIVE` / `NOT_RATIFIED`).
  - `governance/P03_G4_CLASSIFICATION_PLAN.md` is `Ratified / RATIFIED` under `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001`.
  - `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-001` (ratifies `I-1`) and `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-002` (ratifies `I-7`) are canonical at HEAD `1bd5edf8427d7022e141b6a301f96bc2df5fb6b5`.
  - This `I-8` ratification diff.
- non_authorizations:
  - Does **not** ratify any architecture recommendation `R-1..R-6` from `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_EVALUATION_PACKAGE.md`.
  - Does **not** ratify any `ADR-DRAFT-P03-001..006` from `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_EVALUATION_PACKAGE.md`.
  - Does **not** ratify any other implementation-readiness criterion (`I-2`, `I-3`, `I-4`, `I-5`, `I-6`, `I-7`). (Note: `I-1` and `I-7` are already ratified under `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-001` and `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-002` respectively; this decision does not modify or supersede either.)
  - Does **not** modify or supersede `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-001` (the `I-1` row-uniqueness rule).
  - Does **not** modify or supersede `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-002` (the `I-7` explicit-non-authorization disclosure rule).

  - Does **not** authorize implementation, project code, dependency installation, lockfile or manifest changes, license selection, hook registration or activation, settings changes (`.claude/settings.json`, `.claude/settings.local.example.json`), adapter-rule changes (`CLAUDE.md`, `AGENTS.md`, `.claude/rules/**`), runtime context pack generation (`.continuum/RUNTIME_CONTEXT.md`, `.continuum/context-index.yaml`, `.continuum/context-budget.yaml`, `.continuum/context-freshness.yaml`, `.continuum/token-audit.md`), or P04/P05 activation.
  - Does **not** create any P04 or P05 task.

  - Does **not** open P04 GO (source-package Gate G-8). Ratifying `I-8` codifies the P03/P04 separation; it does not authorize, schedule, or initiate P04 activation.
  - Does **not** create or modify `governance/PRODUCT_OWNER.md` (absent and remains absent).
- invariants_preserved:
  - Exactly one active task: `CONT-P03-ARCH-001` (active-task invariant preserved). `I-8` codifies the future closeout-time transition pathway but does not execute that transition.
  - P04 and P05 remain not active; no P04 or P05 task is proposed or activated by this decision.
  - `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001` remains canonical; the G-4 classification set is unchanged.

  - Ratified context-policy set remains canonical and is not superseded.
  - Ratified P02 discovery package and all other ratified governance documents remain canonical and are not superseded.
  - No runtime context pack is generated by this decision.
  - Canonical-wins discipline (P-4): no derived or generated artifact is elevated by this decision.
  - Never-automatic surface (P-9): no automation, hook activation, settings change, or adapter-rule change is implied.

Until such supersession is ratified, the P03 closeout / P04 activation separation discipline binds every future P03 closeout gate and every future P04 activation gate.

The identity `Tural Rahmanli` is not a project identity and must not be encoded as project authority; any incidental appearance of that name in Git committer metadata or environment metadata is not project authority.

## DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-004

- decision_id: `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-004`
- status: `RATIFIED`
- decision: Ratify P03 implementation-readiness criterion `I-2` from `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_EVALUATION_PACKAGE.md` §8 as canonical procedural / ADR-canonicalization discipline under `CONT-P03-ARCH-001`. Ratified criterion text: "every ADR draft in §7 that the Product Owner intends to carry forward has been ratified (or formally modified/split/merged) and its final form is recorded as canonical." Every ADR draft (`ADR-DRAFT-P03-001..006`) that the Product Owner intends to carry forward must therefore be ratified (or formally modified/split/merged) under a separately approved Product Owner gate, and its final canonical form must be recorded as its own canonical `governance/DECISION_LOG.md` row under the `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-NNN` family (or equivalent ratified ADR decision row); ratifying `I-2` does not by itself ratify, modify, split, or merge any ADR draft.
- ratified_by: `Rauf Alizada`
- ratified_at: `2026-06-26`
- source_task: `CONT-P03-ARCH-001`
- source_activation: `DEC-P03-ACTIVATION-001`
- drafted_by: `Claude Code`
- reviewed_by: `Product Owner`
- criterion_ratified: `I-2` (`governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_EVALUATION_PACKAGE.md` §8).
- decision_family: `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-NNN` (per `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_RATIFICATION_PLAN.md` §9). This decision is the fourth row in the `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-NNN` family and is sequenced after `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-001` (which ratified `I-1`), `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-002` (which ratified `I-7`), and `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-003` (which ratified `I-8`).
- related_prior_decisions: `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-003`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-002`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001`, `DEC-P03-ACTIVATION-001`.
- safety_basis:
  - `I-2` is a procedural / ADR-canonicalization discipline rule. It carries no direct content dependency on any unresolved `OQ-P02-*`, `P02-RISK-*`, or `P02-ROAD-*` row.
  - `I-2` does not require modifying `governance/OPEN_QUESTIONS.md`, `governance/RISK_REGISTER.md`, or `governance/ROADMAP.md`.
  - `I-2` does not require revising `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_EVALUATION_PACKAGE.md` or `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_RATIFICATION_PLAN.md`; both remain `PROPOSED_INACTIVE` / `NOT_RATIFIED` as canonical reference framing only.
  - `I-2` does not require modifying or reclassifying any row of `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001`.
  - `I-2` does not by itself ratify, modify, split, or merge any ADR draft (`ADR-DRAFT-P03-001..006`); it only codifies the canonicalization discipline that every ratified ADR carried forward must be recorded as its own canonical decision row under the `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-NNN` family (or equivalent ratified ADR decision row).
  - `I-2` is complementary to `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-001` (`I-1` recommendation row-uniqueness rule), `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-002` (`I-7` explicit-non-authorization disclosure rule), and `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-003` (`I-8` P03 closeout / P04 activation separation rule) and does not conflict with any of them; the four procedural rules co-bind every future P03 ratification gate and every future phase-boundary gate.
- forward_application:
  - Every `ADR-DRAFT-P03-001..006` draft that the Product Owner intends to carry forward must be ratified (or formally modified/split/merged) by a separately approved Product Owner gate, and the ratified ADR must be recorded as its own canonical `governance/DECISION_LOG.md` row under the `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-NNN` family (per `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_RATIFICATION_PLAN.md` §9), or as an equivalent ratified ADR decision row that the Product Owner separately approves. Where a draft is formally modified, split, or merged, the resulting final ADR form (after the formal modification/split/merge) is the canonical form recorded under the same family. A draft that the Product Owner does not intend to carry forward requires no row; ratifying `I-2` does not by itself elevate any draft.
  - The `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-NNN` family rows (or equivalent ratified ADR decision rows) co-apply with `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-001` (`I-1`): the ADR row is itself an architecture decision row and is therefore subject to the row-uniqueness rule.
  - The `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-NNN` family rows (or equivalent ratified ADR decision rows) co-apply with `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-002` (`I-7`): each such row must include an explicit non-authorization / non-scope section enumerating what the ADR decision does not authorize.
  - The `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-NNN` family rows (or equivalent ratified ADR decision rows) co-apply with `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-003` (`I-8`): ratifying an ADR does not by itself open P03 closeout or P04 GO.
  - This forward-application clause restates and binds `I-2`; it does not by itself ratify, modify, split, merge, or carry forward any ADR draft.
- evidence:
  - `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_EVALUATION_PACKAGE.md` §8 carries `I-2` as a proposed implementation-readiness criterion (status: `proposed`; document remains `PROPOSED_INACTIVE` / `NOT_RATIFIED`).
  - `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_RATIFICATION_PLAN.md` §5 lists `I-2` among items ready for procedural ratification planning (document remains `PROPOSED_INACTIVE` / `NOT_RATIFIED`).
  - `governance/P03_G4_CLASSIFICATION_PLAN.md` is `Ratified / RATIFIED` under `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001`.
  - `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-001` (ratifies `I-1`), `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-002` (ratifies `I-7`), and `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-003` (ratifies `I-8`) are canonical at HEAD `a47d5abfaa5c9283dbd3e691dcc62792d3988db0`.
  - This `I-2` ratification diff.
- non_authorizations:
  - Does **not** ratify any architecture recommendation `R-1..R-6` from `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_EVALUATION_PACKAGE.md`.

## DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-001

- decision_id: `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-001`
- status: `RATIFIED`
- decision: Ratify P03 architecture recommendation `R-5` (**Governance-Code Boundary**) from `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_EVALUATION_PACKAGE.md` §6 as canonical architecture posture under `CONT-P03-ARCH-001`. Selected option: **Option B-B (governance-as-contract)** as stated in §6: "adopt Option B-B (governance-as-contract). Rationale: preserves hard separation in spirit while enabling code to validate against governance without writing to it; aligns with `TRUST_BOUNDARIES.md` and the Mutation/Scope-Bound boundary rules." Under this ratification, the governance-code boundary is canonically: code (when any code arrives post-ratified-P04) may read and validate against `governance/` as a contract surface, but may not write to `governance/`; `governance/` remains canonical authority; alternative options `B-A` (hard separation, no code reference) and `B-C` (governance-native annotations) are not adopted. This decision is the first row in the `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-NNN` family.
- ratified_by: `Rauf Alizada`
- ratified_at: `2026-06-26`
- source_task: `CONT-P03-ARCH-001`
- source_activation: `DEC-P03-ACTIVATION-001`
- drafted_by: `Claude Code`
- reviewed_by: `Product Owner`
- recommendation_ratified: `R-5` — Governance-Code Boundary — Option B-B (governance-as-contract) (`governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_EVALUATION_PACKAGE.md` §6).
- decision_family: `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-NNN` (per `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_RATIFICATION_PLAN.md` §9). This decision is the first row in the `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-NNN` family.
- related_prior_decisions: `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-004`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-003`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-002`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001`, `DEC-P03-ACTIVATION-001`.
- safety_basis:
  - `R-5` is the architecture recommendation that selects Option `B-B` for the Governance-Code Boundary dimension. Its dependency surface under the ratified G-4 classification `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001` is exactly one `P03-blocking` `OQ-P02-*` row: `OQ-P02-D-008` (`Reserved Directory` as domain vs repository-mechanics), which per `governance/P03_G4_CLASSIFICATION_PLAN.md` "directly conditions R-5 / ADR-DRAFT-P03-005 (Governance-Code Boundary) on what surfaces are addressable contract surfaces. — Resolved jointly with R-5 / ADR-DRAFT-P03-005 ratification." Ratifying `R-5` with Option `B-B` **bounds** the architecture-level posture of `OQ-P02-D-008` — the governance-code contract surface is now canonically `governance/` (as the contract source) under the canonical-wins rule — without mutating the `OQ-P02-D-008` row in `governance/OPEN_QUESTIONS.md`. Final disposition of `OQ-P02-D-008` (resolution, disposition, or acceptance) remains a separately approved Product Owner gate and is not performed by this decision.
  - `R-5` carries no `P02-RISK-*` `P03-blocking` dependency and no `P02-ROAD-*` `P03-blocking` dependency under `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001`.
  - `R-5` aligns with ratified `governance/TRUST_BOUNDARIES.md` (Mutation / Scope-Bound boundary rules): code may read `governance/` but may not mutate `governance/`; this ratification reinforces, and does not supersede, those boundaries.
  - `R-5` aligns with ratified `governance/CONTEXT_POLICY.md` canonical-wins discipline (P-4): `governance/` remains the single source of authority; any future code reference to `governance/` is subordinate.
  - `R-5` does not by itself ratify `ADR-DRAFT-P03-005` (which mirrors `R-5` content); per `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-004` (`I-2` ADR-canonicalization rule), each ADR draft the Product Owner intends to carry forward requires its own separately approved ratification gate and its own canonical `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-NNN` (or equivalent ratified ADR decision) row.
  - `R-5` does not require revising `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_EVALUATION_PACKAGE.md` or `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_RATIFICATION_PLAN.md`; both remain `PROPOSED_INACTIVE` / `NOT_RATIFIED` as canonical reference framing only.
  - `R-5` is procedurally compliant with `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-001` (`I-1` row-uniqueness rule): this row is the unique `governance/DECISION_LOG.md` row for `R-5`.
  - `R-5` is procedurally compliant with `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-002` (`I-7` explicit-non-authorization disclosure rule): this row carries an explicit `non_authorizations` block (below).
  - `R-5` is procedurally compliant with `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-003` (`I-8` P03 closeout / P04 activation separation rule): ratifying `R-5` does not by itself open P03 closeout or P04 GO.
- forward_application:
  - The Governance-Code Boundary is canonically Option `B-B` (governance-as-contract): when code arrives post-ratified-P04, code may read `governance/` as a contract surface and validate against it, but may not write to `governance/`; `governance/` remains canonical authority and the canonical-wins rule continues to apply on any conflict between code and `governance/`.
  - Any future ADR ratification that elevates `ADR-DRAFT-P03-005` (or its formally modified/split/merged successor) must be consistent with this `R-5` selection of Option `B-B`; an ADR ratification gate that proposes a different option (`B-A`, `B-C`, or any other governance-code boundary posture) is a recommendation revision and requires a separately approved superseding decision under the `DEC-P03-ARCH-REVISION-NNN` family.
  - The bounded posture for `OQ-P02-D-008` is that the canonical contract surface is `governance/` (and, by subordinate extension, the ratified governance documents within it). Final per-row disposition of `OQ-P02-D-008` — including whether `Reserved Directory` is also elevated as a domain concept in any future canonical domain model — remains a separately approved Product Owner gate (per the G-4 reclassification clause of `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001` and the `OQ-P02-*` resolution discipline). This decision does not mutate `governance/OPEN_QUESTIONS.md`.
  - No code, runtime, hook, settings, adapter-rule, dependency, license, or runtime context pack is authorized to act on this boundary at this time. Implementation remains gated by P04 GO.
- evidence:
  - `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_EVALUATION_PACKAGE.md` §6 carries `R-5` with `status: proposed` and the Option `B-B` rationale (document remains `PROPOSED_INACTIVE` / `NOT_RATIFIED`).
  - `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_EVALUATION_PACKAGE.md` §7 carries `ADR-DRAFT-P03-005` mirroring `R-5` (document remains `PROPOSED_INACTIVE` / `NOT_RATIFIED`; ADR draft remains `status: proposed` and is **not** ratified by this decision).
  - `governance/P03_G4_CLASSIFICATION_PLAN.md` is `Ratified / RATIFIED` under `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001`; the `OQ-P02-D-008` row is classified `P03-blocking` with "Resolved jointly with R-5 / ADR-DRAFT-P03-005 ratification."
  - `governance/TRUST_BOUNDARIES.md` is ratified canonical authority and codifies the Mutation / Scope-Bound boundary rules that this recommendation aligns with.
  - `governance/CONTEXT_POLICY.md` is ratified canonical authority and codifies the canonical-wins discipline (P-4) that this recommendation reinforces.
  - `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-002`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-003`, and `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-004` are canonical at HEAD `97ecff0380b4eef75b16ad14f159ec08745a6aa9` and procedurally bind this `R-5` ratification.
  - This `R-5` ratification diff.
- non_authorizations:
  - Does **not** ratify `ADR-DRAFT-P03-005` (Governance-Code Boundary ADR draft). Per `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-004` (`I-2`), ADR ratification requires a separately approved Product Owner gate and its own canonical `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-NNN` (or equivalent) row; ratifying `R-5` does not by itself elevate `ADR-DRAFT-P03-005`.
  - Does **not** ratify any other architecture recommendation (`R-1`, `R-2`, `R-3`, `R-4`, `R-6`) from `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_EVALUATION_PACKAGE.md` §6.
  - Does **not** ratify any other `ADR-DRAFT-P03-001..004` or `ADR-DRAFT-P03-006`.
  - Does **not** ratify any implementation-readiness criterion (`I-3`, `I-4`, `I-5`, `I-6`). (Note: `I-1`, `I-2`, `I-7`, and `I-8` are already ratified under `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-004`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-002`, and `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-003` respectively; this decision does not modify or supersede any of them.)
  - Does **not** modify or supersede `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-002`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-003`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-004`, or `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001`.
  - Does **not** modify or reclassify any row of `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001`; the G-4 classification set is unchanged.
  - Does **not** modify `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_EVALUATION_PACKAGE.md`.
  - Does **not** modify `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_RATIFICATION_PLAN.md`.

## DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-001

- decision_id: `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-001`

The ADR canonicalizes the already-ratified `R-5` posture (`DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-001`) as an ADR decision row, preserving the selected option **Option B-B (governance-as-contract)**. Canonical ADR content (per package §7): context — "when code arrives post-ratified-P04, the boundary between `governance/` and code/runtime/implementation artifacts must be explicit"; decision — "adopt Option B-B (governance-as-contract) per Recommendation R-5"; consequences — "code may read and validate against governance but may not write to `governance/`; governance remains canonical authority; future code references governance contracts explicitly"; alternatives considered — Option B-A (hard separation, no code reference) and Option B-C (governance-native annotations), neither of which is adopted. This decision is the first row in the `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-NNN` family. Governance documents are contract / policy authority only; project code remains separate and requires later explicit implementation authorization (no implementation is authorized by this decision).

## DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-002

- decision_id: `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-002`
- status: `RATIFIED`
- decision: Ratify P03 architecture recommendation `R-1` (**Domain**) from `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_EVALUATION_PACKAGE.md` §6 as canonical architecture posture under `CONT-P03-ARCH-001`. Selected option: **Option D-B (governance-first with thin structured projection)** as stated in §6: "Recommendation R-1 `status: proposed` — **Domain**: adopt Option D-B (governance-first with thin structured projection) once a future Product Owner-approved gate authorizes a derived projection. Rationale: preserves the canonical-wins rule from `CONTEXT_POLICY.md`; matches the candidate-vs-canonical pattern in `DEC-P02-DOMAIN-DISCOVERY-001`; keeps reversibility high." Under this ratification, the canonical Domain Architecture posture is Option `D-B` per §4.1: "Governance markdown remains canonical authority; a small derived structured projection (e.g. an enumerated registry of domain concepts) is generated only with explicit ratification, remains subordinate, and is never authority." Alternative options `D-A` (flat-file governance domain — current trajectory, no separate structured representation) and `D-C` (structured domain model alongside governance) are not adopted. This decision is the second row in the `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-NNN` family, sequenced after `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-001`.
- ratified_by: `Rauf Alizada`
- ratified_at: `2026-06-26`
- source_task: `CONT-P03-ARCH-001`
- source_activation: `DEC-P03-ACTIVATION-001`
- drafted_by: `Claude Code`
- reviewed_by: `Product Owner`
- recommendation_ratified: `R-1` — Domain — Option D-B (governance-first with thin structured projection) (`governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_EVALUATION_PACKAGE.md` §6).
- decision_family: `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-NNN` (per `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_RATIFICATION_PLAN.md` §9). This decision is the second row in the `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-NNN` family, sequenced after `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-001`.
- related_prior_decisions: `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-004`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-003`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-002`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001`, `DEC-P03-ACTIVATION-001`.
- consistency_with_DEC_P03_ARCH_RECO_001_and_DEC_P03_ARCH_ADR_001:
  - `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-001` (which ratified `R-5` with Option `B-B`, governance-as-contract) and `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-001` (which canonicalized `ADR-DRAFT-P03-005` with the same Option `B-B` posture) remain canonical and unchanged. Selecting Option `D-B` for the Domain dimension is internally consistent with the Governance-Code Boundary posture under `B-B` (governance-as-contract): governance markdown remains the canonical authority surface; any derived structured Domain projection introduced under a future ratified gate is subordinate, non-authority, and never elevated above governance — exactly the canonical-wins discipline already adopted in `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-001` / `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-001`.
  - This decision does not re-ratify `R-5`, does not re-ratify `ADR-DRAFT-P03-005`, and does not modify or supersede `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-001` or `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-001`.
- safety_basis:
  - `R-1` is the architecture recommendation that selects Option `D-B` for the Domain dimension. Its dependency surface under the ratified G-4 classification `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001` is, in the Domain dimension itself, exactly one `P03-blocking` `OQ-P02-*` row, one `P03-blocking` `P02-RISK-*` row, and one `P03-blocking` `P02-ROAD-*` row: `OQ-P02-D-001` (`Project` vs `Workspace` as distinct domain concepts vs unified at v1), `P02-RISK-017` (Ambiguous Project / Workspace Scoping), and `P02-ROAD-001` (Resolve Domain-Model Open Questions). Per `governance/P03_G4_CLASSIFICATION_PLAN.md` §5/§6/§7, these three rows are classified `P03-blocking` because each "directly conditions R-1 / ADR-DRAFT-P03-001 (Domain projection scope)" (or, for `P02-ROAD-001`, "covers `OQ-P02-D-*` items classified `P03-blocking`; ratification of R-1 / R-5 / R-6 depends on it"). Ratifying `R-1` with Option `D-B` **bounds** the architecture-level posture of `OQ-P02-D-001` — the canonical Domain authority surface is governance markdown, and any future structured Domain projection (registry, typed model, or similar) is subordinate, generated only under a future separately approved gate, and never elevated to authority — without resolving the `Project` vs `Workspace` semantic question and without mutating the `OQ-P02-D-001` row in `governance/OPEN_QUESTIONS.md`. Final per-row disposition of `OQ-P02-D-001` (including whether `Project` and `Workspace` are ultimately ratified as distinct domain concepts or unified at v1) remains a separately approved Product Owner gate and is not performed by this decision.
  - `P02-RISK-017` (Ambiguous Project / Workspace Scoping) is architecture-posture-**bounded** by this ratification at the canonical authority surface (governance markdown remains the canonical scoping authority surface) without being disposed, accepted, mitigated, transferred, or otherwise transitioned in `governance/RISK_REGISTER.md`. The risk row remains `Proposed; open` until a separately approved Product Owner risk-disposition gate.
  - `P02-ROAD-001` (Resolve Domain-Model Open Questions) is architecture-posture-**bounded** by this ratification at the canonical authority surface (Domain-model resolution proceeds against governance markdown) without being scheduled, started, completed, or otherwise transitioned in `governance/ROADMAP.md`. The roadmap row remains `Proposed; not started` until a separately approved Product Owner roadmap-scheduling gate.
  - Structural cross-cutting `P03-blocking` rows under `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001` — `P02-RISK-001` (Product Owner Authority Confusion / Invalid Identity), `P02-RISK-002` (Active-Task Invariant Violation in P02), `P02-RISK-005` (Unauthorized Commit/Push or Approval-Verb Violation), `P02-RISK-006` (Destructive Git Command Without Explicit Approval), and `P02-RISK-018` (P02 Open Questions Remaining Unresolved Before P03/P04) — are reaffirmed by this ratification: identity discipline (`Rauf Alizada` only) is preserved in this row; the active-task invariant is preserved (`CONT-P03-ARCH-001` remains the single active task); approval-verb discipline is preserved (this is a prepare-diff under separately approved Product Owner approval); destructive-Git discipline is preserved (no destructive Git operation is performed); G-4 classification discipline is preserved (this decision does not reclassify any row of `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001`). These five risk rows are not mutated, disposed, accepted, transferred, or otherwise transitioned in `governance/RISK_REGISTER.md`.
  - `R-1` aligns with ratified `governance/CONTEXT_POLICY.md` canonical-wins discipline (P-4): governance markdown is the single source of canonical Domain authority; any derived Domain projection is subordinate and never elevated.
  - `R-1` aligns with ratified `governance/TRUST_BOUNDARIES.md` (Mutation / Scope-Bound boundary rules): any future Domain projection is a derived artifact and must not mutate or override governance markdown; the canonical authority surface is preserved.
  - `R-1` aligns with the candidate-vs-canonical pattern recorded under `DEC-P02-DOMAIN-DISCOVERY-001`: candidate Domain concepts are surfaced in governance markdown; promotion to canonical status proceeds via Product Owner ratification of governance text, not via any derived artifact.
  - `R-1` does not by itself ratify `ADR-DRAFT-P03-001` (which mirrors `R-1` content for the Domain dimension); per `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-004` (`I-2` ADR-canonicalization rule), each ADR draft the Product Owner intends to carry forward requires its own separately approved ratification gate and its own canonical `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-NNN` (or equivalent ratified ADR decision) row, and when ratified must be consistent with this `R-1` selection of Option `D-B` or be processed as a revision under the `DEC-P03-ARCH-REVISION-NNN` family.
  - `R-1` does not require revising `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_EVALUATION_PACKAGE.md` or `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_RATIFICATION_PLAN.md`; both remain `PROPOSED_INACTIVE` / `NOT_RATIFIED` as canonical reference framing only. (`R-1` is listed in §5 of `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_RATIFICATION_PLAN.md` as ready-for-ratification, not in §6 as requiring revision.)
  - `R-1` is procedurally compliant with `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-001` (`I-1` row-uniqueness rule): this row is the unique `governance/DECISION_LOG.md` row for `R-1`.
  - `R-1` is procedurally compliant with `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-002` (`I-7` explicit-non-authorization disclosure rule): this row carries an explicit `non_authorizations` block (below).
  - `R-1` is procedurally compliant with `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-003` (`I-8` P03 closeout / P04 activation separation rule): ratifying `R-1` does not by itself open P03 closeout or P04 GO.
  - `R-1` is procedurally compliant with `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-004` (`I-2` ADR-canonicalization rule): this row does not by itself ratify any ADR draft; `ADR-DRAFT-P03-001` remains `status: proposed` in `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_EVALUATION_PACKAGE.md` §7 and may be carried forward under a separately approved Product Owner gate as its own canonical row under the `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-NNN` family.
- forward_application:
  - The Domain Architecture is canonically Option `D-B` (governance-first with thin structured projection): governance markdown remains canonical Domain authority; any derived structured projection (registry, typed model, projection artifact, or similar) is subordinate, never authority, generated only under a future separately approved Product Owner ratification gate that defines projection scope, generation rule, freshness rule, and subordination clause.
  - Any future ADR ratification that elevates `ADR-DRAFT-P03-001` (or its formally modified/split/merged successor) must be consistent with this `R-1` selection of Option `D-B`; an ADR ratification gate that proposes a different option (`D-A`, `D-C`, or any other Domain Architecture posture) is a recommendation revision and requires a separately approved superseding decision under the `DEC-P03-ARCH-REVISION-NNN` family.
  - The bounded posture for `OQ-P02-D-001` is that the canonical Domain authority surface is governance markdown, regardless of whether `Project` and `Workspace` are ultimately ratified as distinct domain concepts or unified at v1. Final per-row disposition of `OQ-P02-D-001` (including whether `Project` and `Workspace` are distinct or unified) remains a separately approved Product Owner gate (per the G-4 reclassification clause of `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001` and the `OQ-P02-*` resolution discipline). This decision does not mutate `governance/OPEN_QUESTIONS.md`.

This decision does not mutate `governance/RISK_REGISTER.md`.

This decision does not mutate `governance/ROADMAP.md`.
  - No code, runtime, hook, settings, adapter-rule, dependency, license, or runtime context pack is authorized to act on this Domain posture at this time. Implementation remains gated by P04 GO. Project code remains separate from governance and requires later explicit implementation authorization.

## DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-002

- decision_id: `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-002`
- status: `RATIFIED`
- decision: Canonicalize P03 architecture decision record `ADR-DRAFT-P03-001` (**Domain Representation Strategy**) from `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_EVALUATION_PACKAGE.md` §7 as the canonical Domain Representation Strategy ADR under `CONT-P03-ARCH-001`, consistent with already-ratified `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-002` and preserving the selected Domain option `D-B` (governance-first with thin structured projection). Canonical ADR content (verbatim from §7): "ADR-DRAFT-P03-001 — Domain Representation Strategy. context: `DEC-P02-DOMAIN-DISCOVERY-001` surfaces candidate domain concepts; current state is flat-file. Recommendation R-1 favors Option D-B. decision (proposed): adopt governance-first with thin structured projection (Option D-B) under a future approved gate that defines projection scope, generation rule, freshness rule, and subordination clause. consequences (proposed): introduces a derived projection artifact (subordinate, non-authority); requires a generator path under a future ratified gate; preserves canonical-wins rule. alternatives considered: Option D-A (flat-file only); Option D-C (structured model alongside governance)." Under this ratification the ADR's content moves from `status: proposed` (in the package) to canonical ADR status as a `governance/DECISION_LOG.md` row under the `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-NNN` family; alternative options `D-A` (flat-file governance domain — current trajectory, no separate structured representation) and `D-C` (structured domain model alongside governance) are not adopted. This decision is the second row in the `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-NNN` family, sequenced after `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-001`.
- ratified_by: `Rauf Alizada`
- ratified_at: `2026-06-27`
- source_task: `CONT-P03-ARCH-001`
- source_activation: `DEC-P03-ACTIVATION-001`
- drafted_by: `Claude Code`
- reviewed_by: `Product Owner`
- adr_ratified: `ADR-DRAFT-P03-001` — Domain Representation Strategy (`governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_EVALUATION_PACKAGE.md` §7) — selected Domain option `D-B` (governance-first with thin structured projection) per `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-002`.
- decision_family: `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-NNN` (per `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_RATIFICATION_PLAN.md` §9). This decision is the second row in the `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-NNN` family, sequenced after `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-001`.
- related_prior_decisions: `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-002`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-004`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-003`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-002`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001`, `DEC-P03-ACTIVATION-001`.
- consistency_with_DEC_P03_ARCH_RECO_002_and_DEC_P03_ARCH_RECO_001_and_DEC_P03_ARCH_ADR_001:
  - `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-002` (which ratified `R-1` with Option `D-B`, governance-first with thin structured projection) remains canonical and unchanged. `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-002` canonicalizes the ADR-form expression of the same Domain posture without altering, re-ratifying, modifying, or superseding `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-002`. The canonical Domain Architecture remains Option `D-B`; governance markdown remains canonical Domain authority; any future derived structured Domain projection (registry, typed model, projection artifact, or similar) is subordinate, non-authority, and never elevated to authority — exactly as ratified under `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-002`.
  - `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-001` (which ratified `R-5` with Option `B-B`, governance-as-contract) and `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-001` (which canonicalized `ADR-DRAFT-P03-005` with the same Option `B-B` posture) remain canonical and unchanged. The canonical-wins discipline of `B-B` (governance-as-contract) adopted for the Governance-Code Boundary is preserved here at the ADR level for the Domain dimension: governance markdown remains the canonical authority surface, and the future Domain projection is subordinate and subordinate-only.

- safety_basis:
  - `ADR-DRAFT-P03-001` shares the architecture content of `R-1` and therefore shares the same directly-conditioning `P03-blocking` dependency surface under the ratified G-4 classification `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001`: exactly one `P03-blocking` `OQ-P02-*` row, one `P03-blocking` `P02-RISK-*` row, and one `P03-blocking` `P02-ROAD-*` row — `OQ-P02-D-001` (`Project` vs `Workspace` as distinct domain concepts vs unified at v1), `P02-RISK-017` (Ambiguous Project / Workspace Scoping), and `P02-ROAD-001` (Resolve Domain-Model Open Questions). Per `governance/P03_G4_CLASSIFICATION_PLAN.md` §5/§6/§7 these three rows are classified `P03-blocking` because each directly conditions `R-1` / `ADR-DRAFT-P03-001` on Domain projection scope (or, for `P02-ROAD-001`, covers `OQ-P02-D-*` items classified `P03-blocking` on which `R-1` / `R-5` / `R-6` ratification depends). All three rows are already architecture-posture-**bounded** by `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-002` (canonical Domain authority surface is governance markdown; any future structured Domain projection is subordinate and never elevated to authority). Canonicalizing `ADR-DRAFT-P03-001` under `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-002` **reinforces** the same architecture-posture bound at the ADR level — the canonical Domain ADR records the same governance-first-with-thin-structured-projection posture — without resolving the `Project` vs `Workspace` semantic question and without mutating any of the three rows in `governance/OPEN_QUESTIONS.md`, `governance/RISK_REGISTER.md`, or `governance/ROADMAP.md`. Final per-row disposition of `OQ-P02-D-001` (including whether `Project` and `Workspace` are ultimately ratified as distinct domain concepts or unified at v1), final per-row disposition of `P02-RISK-017`, and final per-row scheduling of `P02-ROAD-001` each remain separately approved Product Owner gates and are not performed by this decision.
  - Structural cross-cutting `P03-blocking` risks `P02-RISK-001`, `P02-RISK-002`, `P02-RISK-005`, `P02-RISK-006`, and `P02-RISK-018` are reaffirmed without mutation; ratifying `ADR-DRAFT-P03-001` at the canonical-Domain-authority surface is consistent with those structural risks remaining canonically open in `governance/RISK_REGISTER.md` until separately disposed.
  - The decision aligns with ratified `governance/CONTEXT_POLICY.md` canonical-wins discipline (P-4), the candidate-vs-canonical pattern established in `DEC-P02-DOMAIN-DISCOVERY-001`, and the canonical-authority-surface discipline of `governance/TRUST_BOUNDARIES.md`.
  - `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-002` satisfies `I-1` (per `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-001`): it is recorded as its own distinct row in `governance/DECISION_LOG.md`, separate from `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-002`.
  - `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-002` satisfies `I-2` (per `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-004`): it is the canonical ADR row for `ADR-DRAFT-P03-001`, recorded under the `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-NNN` family in its final canonical form.
  - `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-002` satisfies `I-7` (per `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-002`): the `non_authorizations:` section below explicitly enumerates what this decision does not authorize.
  - `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-002` preserves `I-8` (per `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-003`): it does not open P03 closeout and does not open P04 GO; both require separately approved Product Owner gates.
- bounded_rows:
  - `OQ-P02-D-001` — architecture-posture-bounded (canonical Domain authority surface is governance markdown; any future structured Domain projection is subordinate and never elevated to authority). The roadmap row remains `Proposed; not started` until a separately approved Product Owner roadmap-scheduling gate.
- forward_application:
  - The canonical Domain Architecture is Option `D-B` (governance-first with thin structured projection), now recorded at both recommendation level (`DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-002`) and ADR level (`DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-002`).

## DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-003

- decision_id: `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-003`
- status: `RATIFIED`
- decision: Ratify P03 architecture recommendation `R-3` (**Data Classification**) from `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_EVALUATION_PACKAGE.md` §6 as canonical architecture posture under `CONT-P03-ARCH-001`. Selected option: **Option C-C (dedicated classification registry)** as stated in §6: "Recommendation R-3 `status: proposed` — **Data Classification**: adopt Option C-C (dedicated classification registry) under a future Product Owner-approved gate; defer Option C-B (per-document frontmatter) unless registry-only proves insufficient. Rationale: centralizes mapping, avoids per-document churn during P03, keeps reversibility high." Under this ratification, the canonical Data Classification Architecture posture is Option `C-C` per §4.3: "A separate ratified document maps each registered governance document to a `data_class` and `sensitivity_level` and records the handling-boundary references; frontmatter remains unchanged." Alternative options `C-A` (implicit classification — current trajectory, class/level mapping lives only in `governance/P02_DATA_CLASSIFICATION_SENSITIVE_BOUNDARY_DRAFT.md` without explicit per-document encoding) and `C-B` (explicit per-document classification frontmatter on governance documents) are not adopted; per §6, Option `C-B` is explicitly **deferred** unless registry-only proves insufficient under a separately approved future gate. This decision is the third row in the `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-NNN` family, sequenced after `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-001` and `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-002`.
- ratified_by: `Rauf Alizada`
- ratified_at: `2026-06-27`
- source_task: `CONT-P03-ARCH-001`
- source_activation: `DEC-P03-ACTIVATION-001`
- drafted_by: `Claude Code`
- reviewed_by: `Product Owner`
- recommendation_ratified: `R-3` — Data Classification — Option C-C (dedicated classification registry) (`governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_EVALUATION_PACKAGE.md` §6).
- decision_family: `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-NNN` (per `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_RATIFICATION_PLAN.md` §9). This decision is the third row in the `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-NNN` family, sequenced after `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-001` and `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-002`.
- related_prior_decisions: `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-002`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-002`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-004`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-003`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-002`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001`, `DEC-P03-ACTIVATION-001`.
- consistency_with_DEC_P03_ARCH_RECO_002_and_DEC_P03_ARCH_RECO_001_and_DEC_P03_ARCH_ADR_001_and_DEC_P03_ARCH_ADR_002:
  - `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-001` (which ratified `R-5` with Option `B-B`, governance-as-contract) and `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-001` (which canonicalized `ADR-DRAFT-P03-005` with the same Option `B-B` posture) remain canonical and unchanged. Selecting Option `C-C` for the Data Classification dimension is internally consistent with the Governance-Code Boundary posture under `B-B` (governance-as-contract): governance markdown remains canonical authority; a separately ratified dedicated classification registry document is itself a governance document subject to the same canonical-wins discipline, and never elevates a derived or generated mapping above canonical authority.
  - `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-002` (which ratified `R-1` with Option `D-B`, governance-first with thin structured projection) and `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-002` (which canonicalized `ADR-DRAFT-P03-001` with the same Option `D-B` posture) remain canonical and unchanged. Selecting Option `C-C` for the Data Classification dimension is internally consistent with the Domain posture under `D-B` (governance-first with thin structured projection): the future dedicated classification registry is a governance-first authority surface — a separately ratified governance document — and any future derived projection from it remains subordinate and never elevated to authority.
  - This decision does not re-ratify `R-1`, `R-5`, `ADR-DRAFT-P03-001`, or `ADR-DRAFT-P03-005`, and does not modify or supersede `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-002`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-001`, or `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-002`.
- safety_basis:
  - `R-3` is the architecture recommendation that selects Option `C-C` for the Data Classification dimension. Its dependency surface under the ratified G-4 classification `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001` covers, in the Data Classification dimension itself, three `P03-blocking` `OQ-P02-*` rows, one `P03-blocking` `P02-RISK-*` row, and one `P03-blocking` `P02-ROAD-*` row: `OQ-P02-C-001` (canonical data classes / sensitivity levels vs deferred), `OQ-P02-C-009` (governance-level validation of handling requirements — **cross-coupled with R-2**), `OQ-P02-C-010` (class-to-sensitivity mapping table), `P02-RISK-016` (undefined canonical data classes / sensitivity levels), and `P02-ROAD-002` (ratify canonical data classes and sensitivity levels). Per `governance/P03_G4_CLASSIFICATION_PLAN.md` §5/§6/§7, these rows are classified `P03-blocking` because each "directly conditions R-3 / ADR-DRAFT-P03-003 (Data Classification realization)" (or, for `P02-ROAD-002`, "drives R-3 / ADR-DRAFT-P03-003 (registry shape) and addresses `P02-RISK-016`").
  - Ratifying `R-3` with Option `C-C` **bounds** the architecture-level posture of `OQ-P02-C-001`, `OQ-P02-C-010`, `P02-RISK-016`, and `P02-ROAD-002` fully — the canonical realization surface for Data Classification is a separately ratified dedicated classification registry document (not implicit text and not per-document frontmatter); the registry shape will map each registered governance document to a `data_class` and `sensitivity_level` and record the handling-boundary references; the canonical class/level vocabulary will be defined inside that registry under its own separately approved Product Owner ratification — without resolving the per-row semantic content of those rows (the specific canonical classes/levels, the specific mapping table, the specific risk disposition, the specific roadmap scheduling) and without mutating any of those rows in `governance/OPEN_QUESTIONS.md`, `governance/RISK_REGISTER.md`, or `governance/ROADMAP.md`. Final per-row disposition / scheduling of each remains a separately approved Product Owner gate.
  - `OQ-P02-C-009` (governance-level validation of handling requirements) is **partially** architecture-posture-bounded by this ratification. Per `governance/P03_G4_CLASSIFICATION_PLAN.md` §5 the row's resolution is "Resolved jointly with R-2 / R-3 revisions and ratifications" — it is **cross-coupled** between the Security/Trust dimension (`R-2`) and the Data Classification dimension (`R-3`). This decision ratifies only `R-3` and therefore bounds the Data Classification portion of `OQ-P02-C-009` only: the canonical handling-requirement surface for documents covered by the future classification registry will be the classification registry itself plus the ratified handling-boundary references it records; governance-level validation of handling requirements remains coupled to a separately approved `R-2` revision and ratification, and `OQ-P02-C-009` is **not** fully bounded by this decision. Final disposition of `OQ-P02-C-009` remains coupled to a separately approved `R-2` revision/ratification gate, and the row is not mutated in `governance/OPEN_QUESTIONS.md` by this decision.
  - `P02-RISK-016` (Undefined Canonical Data Classes / Sensitivity Levels) is architecture-posture-**bounded** by this ratification at the canonical realization surface (the future dedicated classification registry document will define the canonical class/level vocabulary under its own separately approved Product Owner gate) without being disposed, accepted, mitigated, transferred, or otherwise transitioned in `governance/RISK_REGISTER.md`. The risk row remains `Proposed; open` until a separately approved Product Owner risk-disposition gate.
  - `P02-ROAD-002` (Ratify Canonical Data Classes and Sensitivity Levels) is architecture-posture-**bounded** by this ratification at the canonical realization surface (scheduling aligned with the future ratification of the dedicated classification registry) without being scheduled, started, completed, or otherwise transitioned in `governance/ROADMAP.md`. The roadmap row remains `Proposed; not started` until a separately approved Product Owner roadmap-scheduling gate.
  - Structural cross-cutting `P03-blocking` rows under `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001` — `P02-RISK-001` (Product Owner Authority Confusion / Invalid Identity), `P02-RISK-002` (Active-Task Invariant Violation in P02), `P02-RISK-005` (Unauthorized Commit/Push or Approval-Verb Violation), `P02-RISK-006` (Destructive Git Command Without Explicit Approval), and `P02-RISK-018` (P02 Open Questions Remaining Unresolved Before P03/P04) — are reaffirmed by this ratification: identity discipline (`Rauf Alizada` only) is preserved in this row; the active-task invariant is preserved (`CONT-P03-ARCH-001` remains the single active task); approval-verb discipline is preserved (this is a prepare-diff under separately approved Product Owner approval); destructive-Git discipline is preserved (no destructive Git operation is performed); G-4 classification discipline is preserved (this decision does not reclassify any row of `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001`). These five risk rows are not mutated, disposed, accepted, transferred, or otherwise transitioned in `governance/RISK_REGISTER.md`.
  - `R-3` aligns with ratified `governance/CONTEXT_POLICY.md` canonical-wins discipline (P-4): governance markdown is the single source of canonical authority; the future dedicated classification registry is itself a governance document subject to the same canonical-wins rule, and any future derived classification artifact (validator output, projection, or similar) is subordinate and never elevated.
  - `R-3` aligns with ratified `governance/TRUST_BOUNDARIES.md` (Mutation / Scope-Bound boundary rules): the future classification registry is a governance authority surface and does not mutate or override other governance markdown; the registry-only realization avoids per-document churn and centralizes the mapping.
  - `R-3` aligns with `DEC-P02-DATA-CLASSIFICATION-001`: candidate Classes (1..14), Levels (Public/Authority/Evidence/Untrusted/Restricted/Boundary), Bounds (Secret/Identity/Evidence/Context/Scope/External) and the candidate handling requirements surfaced in `governance/P02_DATA_CLASSIFICATION_SENSITIVE_BOUNDARY_DRAFT.md` remain candidate concepts; their canonical promotion (to a final ratified vocabulary) is the proper subject of the future separately approved ratification gate that creates the dedicated classification registry.
  - `R-3` does not by itself ratify `ADR-DRAFT-P03-003` (which mirrors `R-3` content for the Data Classification dimension); per `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-004` (`I-2` ADR-canonicalization rule), each ADR draft the Product Owner intends to carry forward requires its own separately approved ratification gate and its own canonical `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-NNN` (or equivalent ratified ADR decision) row, and when ratified must be consistent with this `R-3` selection of Option `C-C` or be processed as a revision under the `DEC-P03-ARCH-REVISION-NNN` family.
  - `R-3` does not require revising `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_EVALUATION_PACKAGE.md` or `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_RATIFICATION_PLAN.md`; both remain `PROPOSED_INACTIVE` / `NOT_RATIFIED` as canonical reference framing only. (`R-3` is listed in §5 of `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_RATIFICATION_PLAN.md` as ready-for-ratification, not in §6 as requiring revision.)
  - `R-3` is procedurally compliant with `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-001` (`I-1` row-uniqueness rule): this row is the unique `governance/DECISION_LOG.md` row for `R-3`.
  - `R-3` is procedurally compliant with `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-002` (`I-7` explicit-non-authorization disclosure rule): this row carries an explicit `non_authorizations` block (below).
  - `R-3` is procedurally compliant with `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-003` (`I-8` P03 closeout / P04 activation separation rule): ratifying `R-3` does not by itself open P03 closeout or P04 GO.
  - `R-3` is procedurally compliant with `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-004` (`I-2` ADR-canonicalization rule): this row does not by itself ratify any ADR draft; `ADR-DRAFT-P03-003` remains `status: proposed` in `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_EVALUATION_PACKAGE.md` §7 and may be carried forward under a separately approved Product Owner gate as its own canonical row under the `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-NNN` family.
- forward_application:
  - The Data Classification Architecture is canonically Option `C-C` (dedicated classification registry): a future separately ratified governance document will map each registered governance document to a `data_class` and `sensitivity_level` and record the handling-boundary references; frontmatter on existing documents remains unchanged; per-document frontmatter (Option `C-B`) is explicitly **deferred** unless registry-only proves insufficient.
  - Any future ADR ratification that elevates `ADR-DRAFT-P03-003` (or its formally modified/split/merged successor) must be consistent with this `R-3` selection of Option `C-C`; an ADR ratification gate that proposes a different option (`C-A`, `C-B`, or any other Data Classification Architecture posture) is a recommendation revision and requires a separately approved superseding decision under the `DEC-P03-ARCH-REVISION-NNN` family.
  - The bounded posture for `OQ-P02-C-001` is that canonical data classes and sensitivity levels will be ratified inside the future dedicated classification registry document under its own separately approved Product Owner gate; this decision does not enumerate or ratify any specific class/level vocabulary. Final per-row disposition of `OQ-P02-C-001` remains a separately approved Product Owner gate. This decision does not mutate `governance/OPEN_QUESTIONS.md`.
  - The bounded posture for `OQ-P02-C-010` is that the class-to-sensitivity mapping table is realized inside the future dedicated classification registry document under its own separately approved Product Owner gate; this decision does not enumerate or ratify any specific mapping. Final per-row disposition of `OQ-P02-C-010` remains a separately approved Product Owner gate. This decision does not mutate `governance/OPEN_QUESTIONS.md`.
  - The **partially-bounded** posture for `OQ-P02-C-009` is that the Data Classification portion of governance-level validation of handling requirements is realized inside the future dedicated classification registry document (which records handling-boundary references for each registered document); the Security/Trust validation portion remains coupled to a separately approved `R-2` revision and ratification. Final disposition of `OQ-P02-C-009` therefore remains coupled to a separately approved `R-2` revision/ratification gate in addition to the future `R-3` realization gate. This decision does not mutate `governance/OPEN_QUESTIONS.md`.
  - The bounded posture for `P02-RISK-016` is that risk of undefined canonical data classes / sensitivity levels is constrained by the future dedicated classification registry (which will define the canonical vocabulary under its own separately approved ratification gate); risk disposition (accepted-with-mitigation / transferred / mitigated) remains a separately approved Product Owner gate. This decision does not mutate `governance/RISK_REGISTER.md`.
  - The bounded posture for `P02-ROAD-002` is that any roadmap work to ratify canonical data classes and sensitivity levels proceeds against the future dedicated classification registry as the canonical realization surface; scheduling, starting, or completing the roadmap item remains a separately approved Product Owner gate. This decision does not mutate `governance/ROADMAP.md`.
  - No code, runtime, hook, settings, adapter-rule, dependency, license, or runtime context pack is authorized to act on this Data Classification posture at this time. Implementation remains gated by P04 GO. Project code remains separate from governance and requires later explicit implementation authorization.
- evidence:
  - `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_EVALUATION_PACKAGE.md` §4.3 carries `C-A` / `C-B` / `C-C` with `status: proposed`; §6 carries `R-3` with `status: proposed` and the Option `C-C` rationale (defer `C-B` unless registry-only proves insufficient); §7 carries `ADR-DRAFT-P03-003` mirroring `R-3` (document remains `PROPOSED_INACTIVE` / `NOT_RATIFIED`; ADR draft remains `status: proposed` and is **not** ratified by this decision).
  - `governance/P03_G4_CLASSIFICATION_PLAN.md` is `Ratified / RATIFIED` under `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001`; the `OQ-P02-C-001` row is classified `P03-blocking` with rationale "Drives R-3 / ADR-DRAFT-P03-003 (Data Classification realization); registry shape depends on which classes/levels are canonical"; the `OQ-P02-C-009` row is classified `P03-blocking` with rationale "Mirrors `OQ-P02-S-009` for handling requirements; drives R-3 and the Security/Trust evidence threshold under R-2" and is recorded as "Resolved jointly with R-2 / R-3 revisions and ratifications" (the cross-coupled resolution path); the `OQ-P02-C-010` row is classified `P03-blocking` with rationale "Directly conditions the registry shape proposed by R-3 / ADR-DRAFT-P03-003"; the `P02-RISK-016` row is classified `P03-blocking` with rationale "Directly affects R-3 / ADR-DRAFT-P03-003 (Data Classification realization); ratification requires defined canonical labels"; the `P02-ROAD-002` row is classified `P03-blocking` with rationale "Drives R-3 / ADR-DRAFT-P03-003 (registry shape) and addresses `P02-RISK-016`."
  - `governance/CONTEXT_POLICY.md` is ratified canonical authority and codifies the canonical-wins discipline (P-4) that this recommendation reinforces.
  - `governance/TRUST_BOUNDARIES.md` is ratified canonical authority and codifies the Mutation / Scope-Bound boundary rules that this recommendation aligns with.
  - `DEC-P02-DATA-CLASSIFICATION-001` is ratified canonical authority for P02 candidate data classes, sensitivity levels, and sensitive-boundary concepts; candidate vocabulary surfaces remain candidate vocabulary until the future dedicated classification registry promotes them under its own separately approved Product Owner ratification.
  - `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-002`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-003`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-004`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-002`, and `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-002` are canonical at HEAD `71561e045ade680a35e626d5d3f4a755a2f605dd` and procedurally bind this `R-3` ratification.
  - This `R-3` ratification diff.
- non_authorizations:
  - Does **not** ratify `ADR-DRAFT-P03-003` (Data Classification ADR draft). Per `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-004` (`I-2`), ADR ratification requires a separately approved Product Owner gate and its own canonical `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-NNN` (or equivalent) row; ratifying `R-3` does not by itself elevate `ADR-DRAFT-P03-003`. `ADR-DRAFT-P03-003` remains a separate possible later ADR ratification path.
  - Does **not** ratify `R-2`, `R-4`, or `R-6`.

## DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-003

- decision_id: `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-003`
- status: `RATIFIED`
- decision: Canonicalize P03 architecture decision record `ADR-DRAFT-P03-003` (**Data Classification Realization**) from `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_EVALUATION_PACKAGE.md` §7 as the canonical Data Classification ADR under `CONT-P03-ARCH-001`, consistent with already-ratified `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-003` and preserving the selected Data Classification option `C-C` (dedicated classification registry). Canonical ADR content (verbatim from §7): "ADR-DRAFT-P03-003 — Data Classification Realization. context: `DEC-P02-DATA-CLASSIFICATION-001` defines candidate Classes (1..14), Levels (Public/Authority/Evidence/Untrusted/Restricted/Boundary), and Bounds (Secret/Identity/Evidence/Context/Scope/External). decision (proposed): adopt Option C-C (dedicated classification registry) under a future approved gate; defer Option C-B unless registry-only proves insufficient (Recommendation R-3). consequences (proposed): adds one ratified registry artifact; documents map to class/level via the registry; per-document frontmatter churn avoided in P03. alternatives considered: Option C-A (implicit classification only); Option C-B (per-document frontmatter)." Under this ratification the ADR's content moves from `status: proposed` (in the package) to canonical ADR status as a `governance/DECISION_LOG.md` row under the `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-NNN` family; alternative options `C-A` (implicit classification — current trajectory, class/level mapping lives only in `governance/P02_DATA_CLASSIFICATION_SENSITIVE_BOUNDARY_DRAFT.md` without explicit per-document encoding) and `C-B` (explicit per-document classification frontmatter on governance documents) are not adopted; Option `C-B` per-document frontmatter remains explicitly **deferred** unless registry-only proves insufficient under a separately approved future gate. This decision is the third row in the `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-NNN` family, sequenced after `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-001` and `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-002`. This ADR ratification canonicalizes the already-ratified `R-3` posture (under `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-003`) as an ADR decision; it does not re-ratify `R-3` as a recommendation.
- ratified_by: `Rauf Alizada`
- ratified_at: `2026-06-27`
- source_task: `CONT-P03-ARCH-001`
- source_activation: `DEC-P03-ACTIVATION-001`
- drafted_by: `Claude Code`
- reviewed_by: `Product Owner`
- adr_ratified: `ADR-DRAFT-P03-003` — Data Classification Realization (`governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_EVALUATION_PACKAGE.md` §7) — selected Data Classification option `C-C` (dedicated classification registry) per `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-003`.
- decision_family: `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-NNN` (per `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_RATIFICATION_PLAN.md` §9). This decision is the third row in the `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-NNN` family, sequenced after `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-001` and `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-002`.
- related_prior_decisions: `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-003`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-002`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-002`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-004`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-003`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-002`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001`, `DEC-P03-ACTIVATION-001`.
- consistency_with_DEC_P03_ARCH_RECO_003_and_DEC_P03_ARCH_RECO_002_and_DEC_P03_ARCH_RECO_001_and_DEC_P03_ARCH_ADR_001_and_DEC_P03_ARCH_ADR_002:
  - `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-003` (which ratified `R-3` with Option `C-C`, dedicated classification registry) remains canonical and unchanged. `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-003` canonicalizes the ADR-form expression of the same Data Classification posture without altering, re-ratifying, modifying, or superseding `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-003`. The canonical Data Classification Architecture remains Option `C-C`; the future separately ratified dedicated classification registry document is the canonical realization surface (mapping each registered governance document to a `data_class` and `sensitivity_level` and recording the handling-boundary references); per-document frontmatter remains unchanged; per-document frontmatter (Option `C-B`) remains explicitly **deferred** unless registry-only proves insufficient under a separately approved future gate — exactly as ratified under `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-003`.
  - `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-001` (which ratified `R-5` with Option `B-B`, governance-as-contract) and `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-001` (which canonicalized `ADR-DRAFT-P03-005` with the same Option `B-B` posture) remain canonical and unchanged. The canonical-wins discipline of `B-B` (governance-as-contract) is preserved here at the ADR level for the Data Classification dimension: the future dedicated classification registry is itself a governance document subject to the same canonical-wins discipline, and any future derived classification artifact (validator output, projection, or similar) is subordinate and never elevated to authority.
  - `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-002` (which ratified `R-1` with Option `D-B`, governance-first with thin structured projection) and `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-002` (which canonicalized `ADR-DRAFT-P03-001` with the same Option `D-B` posture) remain canonical and unchanged. The governance-first authority surface of `D-B` is preserved here at the ADR level for the Data Classification dimension: the future dedicated classification registry is a governance-first authority surface — a separately ratified governance document — and any future derived projection from it remains subordinate and never elevated to authority.
  - This decision does not re-ratify `R-3`, `R-1`, `R-5`, `ADR-DRAFT-P03-001`, or `ADR-DRAFT-P03-005`, and does not modify or supersede `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-002`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-003`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-001`, or `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-002`.
- safety_basis:
  - `ADR-DRAFT-P03-003` shares the architecture content of `R-3` and therefore shares the same directly-conditioning `P03-blocking` dependency surface under the ratified G-4 classification `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001`: three `P03-blocking` `OQ-P02-*` rows, one `P03-blocking` `P02-RISK-*` row, and one `P03-blocking` `P02-ROAD-*` row in the Data Classification dimension — `OQ-P02-C-001` (canonical data classes / sensitivity levels vs deferred), `OQ-P02-C-009` (governance-level validation of handling requirements — **cross-coupled with `R-2`**), `OQ-P02-C-010` (class-to-sensitivity mapping table), `P02-RISK-016` (Undefined Canonical Data Classes / Sensitivity Levels), and `P02-ROAD-002` (Ratify Canonical Data Classes and Sensitivity Levels). Per `governance/P03_G4_CLASSIFICATION_PLAN.md` §5/§6/§7 these rows are classified `P03-blocking` because each "directly conditions R-3 / ADR-DRAFT-P03-003 (Data Classification realization)" (or, for `P02-ROAD-002`, "drives R-3 / ADR-DRAFT-P03-003 (registry shape) and addresses `P02-RISK-016`").
  - `OQ-P02-C-001`, `OQ-P02-C-010`, `P02-RISK-016`, and `P02-ROAD-002` are already architecture-posture-**bounded** by `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-003` (canonical realization surface is the future separately ratified dedicated classification registry document). Canonicalizing `ADR-DRAFT-P03-003` under `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-003` **reinforces** the same architecture-posture bound at the ADR level — the canonical Data Classification ADR records the same dedicated-classification-registry posture — without resolving the per-row semantic content of those rows (the specific canonical classes/levels, the specific mapping table, the specific risk disposition, the specific roadmap scheduling) and without mutating any of those rows in `governance/OPEN_QUESTIONS.md`, `governance/RISK_REGISTER.md`, or `governance/ROADMAP.md`. Final per-row disposition of `OQ-P02-C-001`, final per-row disposition of `OQ-P02-C-010`, final per-row disposition of `P02-RISK-016`, and final per-row scheduling of `P02-ROAD-002` each remain separately approved Product Owner gates and are not performed by this decision.
  - `OQ-P02-C-009` (governance-level validation of handling requirements) is only **partially** architecture-posture-reinforced-bounded by this ADR ratification for the Data Classification dimension. Per `governance/P03_G4_CLASSIFICATION_PLAN.md` §5 the row's resolution is "Resolved jointly with R-2 / R-3 revisions and ratifications" — it is **cross-coupled** between the Security/Trust dimension (`R-2`) and the Data Classification dimension (`R-3`). Already partially bounded by `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-003` for the Data Classification dimension only; `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-003` reinforces the Data Classification portion of that bound at the ADR level (the canonical handling-requirement surface for documents covered by the future classification registry will be the classification registry itself plus the ratified handling-boundary references it records). The Security/Trust validation portion of `OQ-P02-C-009` is **not** bounded by this ADR ratification; final disposition of `OQ-P02-C-009` remains coupled to a separately approved `R-2` revision/ratification gate and a separate Product Owner source-register follow-up gate. The row is not mutated in `governance/OPEN_QUESTIONS.md` by this decision.
  - Structural cross-cutting `P03-blocking` risks `P02-RISK-001`, `P02-RISK-002`, `P02-RISK-005`, `P02-RISK-006`, and `P02-RISK-018` are reaffirmed without mutation; ratifying `ADR-DRAFT-P03-003` at the canonical-Data-Classification-ADR surface is consistent with those structural risks remaining canonically open in `governance/RISK_REGISTER.md` until separately disposed.
  - The decision aligns with ratified `governance/CONTEXT_POLICY.md` canonical-wins discipline (P-4), ratified `governance/TRUST_BOUNDARIES.md` Mutation / Scope-Bound boundary rules, the candidate-vs-canonical pattern established in `DEC-P02-DATA-CLASSIFICATION-001`, and the canonical-authority-surface discipline of `governance/TRUST_BOUNDARIES.md`.
  - `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-003` satisfies `I-1` (per `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-001`): it is recorded as its own distinct row in `governance/DECISION_LOG.md`, separate from `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-003`.
  - `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-003` satisfies `I-2` (per `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-004`): it is the canonical ADR row for `ADR-DRAFT-P03-003`, recorded under the `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-NNN` family in its final canonical form.
  - `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-003` satisfies `I-7` (per `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-002`): the `non_authorizations:` section below explicitly enumerates what this decision does not authorize.
  - `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-003` preserves `I-8` (per `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-003`): it does not open P03 closeout and does not open P04 GO; both require separately approved Product Owner gates.
- bounded_rows:
  - `OQ-P02-C-001` — architecture-posture-bounded (canonical realization surface is the future separately ratified dedicated classification registry document; the canonical class/level vocabulary will be defined inside that registry under its own separately approved Product Owner gate). Already bounded by `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-003`; reinforced at ADR level by `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-003`. Source register `governance/OPEN_QUESTIONS.md` remains unchanged. Final per-row disposition remains a separately approved Product Owner gate.

Final per-row disposition remains a separately approved Product Owner gate.
  - `OQ-P02-C-009` — architecture-posture-**partially**-bounded for the Data Classification dimension only (the future dedicated classification registry records handling-boundary references for each registered document; the Security/Trust validation portion of governance-level validation of handling requirements remains coupled to a separately approved `R-2` revision/ratification gate). Already partially bounded by `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-003`; reinforced at ADR level by `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-003` for the Data Classification portion only. Source register `governance/OPEN_QUESTIONS.md` remains unchanged. Final disposition of `OQ-P02-C-009` remains coupled to a separately approved `R-2` revision/ratification gate and a separate Product Owner source-register follow-up gate.
  - `P02-RISK-016` — architecture-posture-bounded at the canonical realization surface (the future dedicated classification registry document will define the canonical class/level vocabulary under its own separately approved Product Owner gate). Already bounded by `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-003`; reinforced at ADR level by `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-003`. Source register `governance/RISK_REGISTER.md` remains unchanged. Risk disposition (accepted-with-mitigation / transferred / mitigated) remains a separately approved Product Owner gate. The risk row remains `Proposed; open`.
  - `P02-ROAD-002` — architecture-posture-bounded at the canonical realization surface (scheduling aligned with the future ratification of the dedicated classification registry). Already bounded by `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-003`; reinforced at ADR level by `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-003`. Source register `governance/ROADMAP.md` remains unchanged. The roadmap row remains `Proposed; not started` until a separately approved Product Owner roadmap-scheduling gate.
- forward_application:
  - The canonical Data Classification Architecture is Option `C-C` (dedicated classification registry), now recorded at both recommendation level (`DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-003`) and ADR level (`DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-003`).
  - Any future ratified generator, validator, or projection from the dedicated classification registry artifact (registry-derived check, projection artifact, automated mapping consumer, or similar) must be authorized by a separately approved Product Owner gate, and the artifact must remain subordinate and never elevated to authority.
  - Creation, generation, population, and registration of the future dedicated classification registry document itself remain separately approved Product Owner gates that must explicitly define the canonical class/level vocabulary, the document-to-class mapping table, the handling-boundary references, and the subordination clause.
  - Any future ADR revision affecting `ADR-DRAFT-P03-003` requires a `DEC-P03-ARCH-REVISION-NNN` decision and must remain consistent with `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-003` (or be paired with explicit supersession/revision of `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-003`).
