  - Does **not** accept, dispose, mitigate, transfer, or otherwise transition any `P02-RISK-*` row in the source register.
  - Does **not** schedule, start, complete, or otherwise transition any `P02-ROAD-*` item in the source register.

Such creation requires a separately approved Product Owner gate that defines the canonical class/level vocabulary, the document-to-class mapping table, the handling-boundary references, and the subordination clause.

  - Does **not** authorize P04 or P05 activation, and does **not** create any P04 or P05 task.

  - Does **not** open P04 GO (source-package Gate G-8).

  - `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-002`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-003`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-004`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-002`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-002`, and `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-003` remain canonical and unsuperseded.

  - Canonical-wins discipline (P-4): no derived or generated artifact is elevated by this decision; the future dedicated classification registry is a governance document subject to the same canonical-wins discipline.
  - Never-automatic surface (P-9): no automation, hook activation, settings change, or adapter-rule change is implied.
- reversibility: A future Product Owner decision may supersede `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-003` by introducing a successor `DEC-P03-ARCH-REVISION-NNN` row (or a successor `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-NNN` row that explicitly supersedes this decision) that revises the canonical Data Classification ADR. Any such revision must remain consistent with `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-003` (Option `C-C`) or be paired with explicit supersession or revision of `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-003`.

Does **not** re-ratify `R-3`, ratify any other recommendation (`R-2`, `R-4`, `R-6`), re-ratify `R-1` or `R-5`, ratify any other ADR (`ADR-DRAFT-P03-002`, `ADR-DRAFT-P03-004`, `ADR-DRAFT-P03-006`), re-ratify `ADR-DRAFT-P03-001` or `ADR-DRAFT-P03-005`, ratify any other criterion (`I-3`, `I-4`, `I-5`, `I-6`), modify or supersede `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-002`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-003`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-002`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-001..004`, or `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001`, modify the proposed P03 evaluation package, proposed P03 ratification plan, or ratified P03 G-4 classification record, mutate any source register (`OQ-P02-C-001`, `OQ-P02-C-010`, `P02-RISK-016`, `P02-ROAD-002` reinforced-bounded but not mutated; `OQ-P02-C-009` reinforced-partially-bounded for Data Classification only but not mutated, with final disposition coupled to a separately approved `R-2` revision/ratification gate; `OQ-P02-D-001`, `P02-RISK-017`, `P02-ROAD-001`, `OQ-P02-D-008` not affected by this decision), create or generate any dedicated classification registry file/artifact, ratify any canonical data class or sensitivity level vocabulary, modify or add frontmatter to any governance document (Option `C-B` per-document frontmatter is explicitly deferred), authorize implementation, open P03 closeout, or open P04 GO. Subsequent per-recommendation, per-ADR, per-criterion, per-row, P03-closeout, and P04-activation ratification gates remain separately required.

## DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-004

- decision_id: `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-004`
- status: `RATIFIED`
- decision: Ratify P03 architecture recommendation `R-6` (**Agent-Adapter Boundary**) from `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_EVALUATION_PACKAGE.md` §6 as canonical architecture posture under `CONT-P03-ARCH-001`. Selected option: **Option A-C (adapter abstraction via a future `ADAPTER_CONTRACT.md`-like artifact)** as stated in §6: "Recommendation R-6 `status: proposed` — **Agent-Adapter Boundary**: adopt Option A-C (adapter abstraction via a future `ADAPTER_CONTRACT.md`-like artifact), starting from the existing single adapter (Option A-A) and introducing a formal contract under a separately approved gate before any second adapter is added. Rationale: keeps governance single-sourced; makes adapter subordination explicit; supports future multi-adapter evolution without ad-hoc divergence." Under this ratification, the canonical Agent-Adapter Boundary Architecture posture is Option `A-C` per §4.6: "Option A-C `status: proposed` — **Adapter abstraction layer**. A small vendor-neutral adapter contract (e.g. an `ADAPTER_CONTRACT.md`) defines required adapter behaviors (cold-start reading, authority order, approval-verb discipline, never-automatic surface), and each vendor adapter implements that contract; governance remains single-sourced." The selection is staged from the existing Option `A-A` single-adapter state (`CLAUDE.md` + `.claude/rules/**` + `.claude/skills/**` + `.claude/agents/**` + `.claude/hooks/**` + `.claude/settings.json` + `.claude/settings.local.example.json` as the only adapter surface today); a formal adapter contract is introduced under a separately approved Product Owner gate before any second vendor adapter is added. Alternative options `A-A` (single adapter indefinitely — current trajectory carried forward without contract abstraction) and `A-B` (multi-adapter with shared governance but without a formal contract — additional adapter entry points such as `AGENTS.md` plus a vendor-specific subdirectory added under separately approved gates, governance remains single-sourced, adapter rules remain subordinate behavioral guidance) are not adopted as the canonical posture; per §6, Option `A-A` continues as the *interim* surface only until a formal `ADAPTER_CONTRACT.md`-like artifact is separately ratified, and Option `A-B` (multi-adapter without a formal contract) is not adopted at any horizon under this decision. This decision is the fourth row in the `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-NNN` family, sequenced after `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-002`, and `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-003`.
- ratified_by: `Rauf Alizada`
- ratified_at: `2026-06-27`
- source_task: `CONT-P03-ARCH-001`
- source_activation: `DEC-P03-ACTIVATION-001`
- drafted_by: `Claude Code`
- reviewed_by: `Product Owner`
- recommendation_ratified: `R-6` — Agent-Adapter Boundary — Option A-C (adapter abstraction via a future `ADAPTER_CONTRACT.md`-like artifact) (`governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_EVALUATION_PACKAGE.md` §6).
- decision_family: `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-NNN` (per `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_RATIFICATION_PLAN.md` §9). This decision is the fourth row in the `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-NNN` family, sequenced after `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-002`, and `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-003`.
- related_prior_decisions: `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-003`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-003`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-002`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-002`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-004`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-003`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-002`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001`, `DEC-P03-ACTIVATION-001`.
- consistency_with_DEC_P03_ARCH_RECO_003_and_DEC_P03_ARCH_ADR_003_and_DEC_P03_ARCH_RECO_002_and_DEC_P03_ARCH_ADR_002_and_DEC_P03_ARCH_RECO_001_and_DEC_P03_ARCH_ADR_001:
  - `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-001` (which ratified `R-5` with Option `B-B`, governance-as-contract) and `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-001` (which canonicalized `ADR-DRAFT-P03-005` with the same Option `B-B` posture) remain canonical and unchanged. Selecting Option `A-C` for the Agent-Adapter Boundary dimension is internally consistent with the Governance-Code Boundary posture under `B-B` (governance-as-contract): governance markdown remains canonical authority; the future vendor-neutral adapter contract (e.g. `ADAPTER_CONTRACT.md`) is itself a governance document subject to the same canonical-wins discipline, and vendor adapters (current Claude Code adapter and any future adapter) remain subordinate behavioral guidance that implements — but never elevates above — that governance contract.
  - `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-002` (which ratified `R-1` with Option `D-B`, governance-first with thin structured projection) and `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-002` (which canonicalized `ADR-DRAFT-P03-001` with the same Option `D-B` posture) remain canonical and unchanged. Selecting Option `A-C` for the Agent-Adapter Boundary dimension is internally consistent with the Domain posture under `D-B`: the future adapter contract is a governance-first authority surface — a separately ratified governance document — and any future derived projection of agent identity, agent behavior, or adapter mapping remains subordinate and never elevated to authority.
  - `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-003` (which ratified `R-3` with Option `C-C`, dedicated classification registry) and `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-003` (which canonicalized `ADR-DRAFT-P03-003` with the same Option `C-C` posture) remain canonical and unchanged. Selecting Option `A-C` for the Agent-Adapter Boundary dimension is internally consistent with the Data Classification posture under `C-C`: both posture choices share the same pattern — a separately ratified governance document records canonical content (classification registry for `R-3`/`ADR-003`; adapter contract for `R-6`) and existing per-document or per-adapter surfaces remain unchanged until that separately ratified document is introduced under its own Product Owner gate.
  - This decision does not re-ratify `R-1`, `R-3`, `R-5`, `ADR-DRAFT-P03-001`, `ADR-DRAFT-P03-003`, or `ADR-DRAFT-P03-005`, and does not modify or supersede `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-002`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-003`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-002`, or `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-003`.
- safety_basis:
  - `R-6` is the architecture recommendation that selects Option `A-C` for the Agent-Adapter Boundary dimension. Its dependency surface under the ratified G-4 classification `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001` covers, in the Agent-Adapter Boundary dimension itself, two `P03-blocking` `OQ-P02-*` rows and one `P03-blocking` `P02-ROAD-*` row: `OQ-P02-D-007` (Agent as domain concept vs adapter/runtime concern), `OQ-P02-S-005` (Agent-behavior split between governance and adapter rules), and `P02-ROAD-009` (Decide Adapter-Rule vs Governance Split for Agent Behavior). Per `governance/P03_G4_CLASSIFICATION_PLAN.md` §5/§7, these rows are classified `P03-blocking` because each "directly conditions R-6 / ADR-DRAFT-P03-006 (Agent-Adapter Boundary)" (or, for `P02-ROAD-009`, "drives R-6 / ADR-DRAFT-P03-006 (Agent-Adapter Boundary)").
  - Ratifying `R-6` with Option `A-C` **bounds** the architecture-level posture of `OQ-P02-D-007`, `OQ-P02-S-005`, and `P02-ROAD-009` fully — the canonical realization surface for the Agent-Adapter Boundary is a future separately ratified vendor-neutral adapter contract document (`ADAPTER_CONTRACT.md`-like artifact) that defines required adapter behaviors (cold-start reading, authority order, approval-verb discipline, never-automatic surface); the canonical split between agent-as-governance-concept and agent-as-adapter-concept will be expressed inside that contract document (Agent identity, Agent authority order, Agent approval-verb discipline, Agent never-automatic surface, and any other agent-shaped contract terms remain enumerated inside the future contract under its own separately approved Product Owner ratification); the canonical adapter-rule-vs-governance-split for agent behavior will likewise be expressed inside that contract — without resolving the per-row semantic content of those rows (the specific contract clauses, the specific behavior split, the specific roadmap scheduling) and without mutating any of those rows in `governance/OPEN_QUESTIONS.md` or `governance/ROADMAP.md`. Final per-row disposition / scheduling of each remains a separately approved Product Owner gate.
  - `P02-RISK-007` (Hook / Adapter / Settings Drift Before Ratified Gate) is **partially** architecture-posture-bounded by this ratification. Per `governance/P03_G4_CLASSIFICATION_PLAN.md` §6 the row's resolution is "Resolved jointly with R-2 / R-6 ratifications" — it is **cross-coupled** between the Security/Trust dimension (`R-2`) and the Agent-Adapter Boundary dimension (`R-6`). This decision ratifies only `R-6` and therefore bounds the Agent-Adapter Boundary portion of `P02-RISK-007` only: the canonical adapter-rule and settings surface for the future adapter contract will be the contract itself plus the subordination clause it records (vendor adapters remain subordinate behavioral guidance; adapter rules and settings remain non-authoritative against governance); hook activation, hook drift, and settings drift relative to the ratified hook-activation discipline remain coupled to a separately approved `R-2` ratification, and `P02-RISK-007` is **not** fully bounded by this decision. Final disposition of `P02-RISK-007` remains coupled to a separately approved `R-2` ratification gate and a separate Product Owner risk-disposition gate, and the row is not mutated in `governance/RISK_REGISTER.md` by this decision.
  - `P02-ROAD-001` (Resolve Domain-Model Open Questions) is already architecture-posture-**bounded** by `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-002` and reinforced at ADR level by `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-002` for the Domain dimension (R-1 / Option `D-B`). Per `governance/P03_G4_CLASSIFICATION_PLAN.md` §7 the row's dimension is "Cross-cutting (Domain + Governance-Code + Agent-Adapter)" and its scheduling is "Scheduling aligned with R-1 / R-5 / R-6 ratifications". `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-004` **reinforces** the row for the Agent-Adapter Boundary dependency surface only — the canonical realization surface for the Agent-Adapter portion of `P02-ROAD-001`'s scheduling is the future separately ratified adapter contract document (the same canonical realization surface that bounds `OQ-P02-D-007`, `OQ-P02-S-005`, and `P02-ROAD-009`) — without modifying the Domain-dimension bound already established by `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-002` / `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-002` and without addressing the Governance-Code dimension (which remains coupled to a separately approved `R-5`-related follow-up if any). This decision does not mutate `governance/ROADMAP.md`; final scheduling of `P02-ROAD-001` remains a separately approved Product Owner roadmap-scheduling gate.
  - Structural cross-cutting `P03-blocking` rows under `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001` — `P02-RISK-001` (Product Owner Authority Confusion / Invalid Identity), `P02-RISK-002` (Active-Task Invariant Violation in P02), `P02-RISK-005` (Unauthorized Commit/Push or Approval-Verb Violation), `P02-RISK-006` (Destructive Git Command Without Explicit Approval), and `P02-RISK-018` (P02 Open Questions Remaining Unresolved Before P03/P04) — are reaffirmed by this ratification: identity discipline (`Rauf Alizada` only) is preserved in this row; the active-task invariant is preserved (`CONT-P03-ARCH-001` remains the single active task); approval-verb discipline is preserved (this is a prepare-diff under separately approved Product Owner approval); destructive-Git discipline is preserved (no destructive Git operation is performed); G-4 classification discipline is preserved (this decision does not reclassify any row of `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001`). These five risk rows are not mutated, disposed, accepted, transferred, or otherwise transitioned in `governance/RISK_REGISTER.md`.
  - `R-6` aligns with ratified `governance/CONTEXT_POLICY.md` canonical-wins discipline (P-4): governance markdown is the single source of canonical authority; the future vendor-neutral adapter contract is itself a governance document subject to the same canonical-wins rule, and any future derived adapter artifact (per-vendor adapter file, projection, or similar) is subordinate and never elevated.
  - `R-6` aligns with ratified `governance/TRUST_BOUNDARIES.md` (Mutation / Scope-Bound boundary rules): the future adapter contract is a governance authority surface and does not mutate or override other governance markdown; vendor adapters (current `CLAUDE.md` / `.claude/rules/**` Claude Code adapter and any future vendor adapter) remain subordinate behavioral guidance only.
  - `R-6` does not by itself ratify `ADR-DRAFT-P03-006` (which mirrors `R-6` content for the Agent-Adapter Boundary dimension); per `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-004` (`I-2` ADR-canonicalization rule), each ADR draft the Product Owner intends to carry forward requires its own separately approved ratification gate and its own canonical `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-NNN` (or equivalent ratified ADR decision) row, and when ratified must be consistent with this `R-6` selection of Option `A-C` or be processed as a revision under the `DEC-P03-ARCH-REVISION-NNN` family.
  - `R-6` does not require revising `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_EVALUATION_PACKAGE.md` or `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_RATIFICATION_PLAN.md`; both remain `PROPOSED_INACTIVE` / `NOT_RATIFIED` as canonical reference framing only. (`R-6` is listed in §5 of `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_RATIFICATION_PLAN.md` as ready-for-ratification, not in §6 as requiring revision.)
  - `R-6` is procedurally compliant with `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-001` (`I-1` row-uniqueness rule): this row is the unique `governance/DECISION_LOG.md` row for `R-6`.
  - `R-6` is procedurally compliant with `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-002` (`I-7` explicit-non-authorization disclosure rule): this row carries an explicit `non_authorizations` block (below).
  - `R-6` is procedurally compliant with `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-003` (`I-8` P03 closeout / P04 activation separation rule): ratifying `R-6` does not by itself open P03 closeout or P04 GO.
  - `R-6` is procedurally compliant with `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-004` (`I-2` ADR-canonicalization rule): this row does not by itself ratify any ADR draft; `ADR-DRAFT-P03-006` remains `status: proposed` in `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_EVALUATION_PACKAGE.md` §7 and may be carried forward under a separately approved Product Owner gate as its own canonical row under the `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-NNN` family.
- forward_application:
  - The Agent-Adapter Boundary Architecture is canonically Option `A-C` (adapter abstraction layer): a future separately ratified vendor-neutral adapter contract document (e.g. `ADAPTER_CONTRACT.md`) will define required adapter behaviors (cold-start reading, authority order, approval-verb discipline, never-automatic surface); the current Claude Code adapter surface (`CLAUDE.md` + `.claude/rules/**` + `.claude/skills/**` + `.claude/agents/**` + `.claude/hooks/**` + `.claude/settings.json` + `.claude/settings.local.example.json`) remains the only adapter surface in effect (Option `A-A` interim state) until that separately ratified contract is introduced under a separately approved Product Owner gate; a second vendor adapter may not be added until the contract is ratified.
  - Any future ADR ratification that elevates `ADR-DRAFT-P03-006` (or its formally modified/split/merged successor) must be consistent with this `R-6` selection of Option `A-C`; an ADR ratification gate that proposes a different option (`A-A` indefinitely, `A-B` multi-adapter without a contract, or any other Agent-Adapter Boundary posture) is a recommendation revision and requires a separately approved superseding decision under the `DEC-P03-ARCH-REVISION-NNN` family.
  - The bounded posture for `OQ-P02-D-007` is that the question of `Agent` as domain concept vs adapter/runtime concern is canonically resolved inside the future separately ratified adapter contract document — agent identity, agent authority order, agent approval-verb discipline, and agent never-automatic surface are recorded as contract terms in that document under its own separately approved Product Owner gate; this decision does not enumerate or ratify any specific agent contract clause. Final per-row disposition of `OQ-P02-D-007` remains a separately approved Product Owner gate. This decision does not mutate `governance/OPEN_QUESTIONS.md`.
  - The bounded posture for `OQ-P02-S-005` is that the canonical agent-behavior split between governance and adapter rules is expressed inside the future separately ratified adapter contract document — the contract defines which behaviors are governance-canonical, which behaviors are adapter-rule behavioral guidance, and how vendor adapters implement the contract; this decision does not enumerate or ratify any specific split. Final per-row disposition of `OQ-P02-S-005` remains a separately approved Product Owner gate. This decision does not mutate `governance/OPEN_QUESTIONS.md`.
  - The bounded posture for `P02-ROAD-009` is that any roadmap work to decide the adapter-rule vs governance split for agent behavior proceeds against the future separately ratified adapter contract document as the canonical realization surface; scheduling, starting, or completing the roadmap item remains a separately approved Product Owner gate. This decision does not mutate `governance/ROADMAP.md`.
  - The **partially-bounded** posture for `P02-RISK-007` is that the Agent-Adapter Boundary portion of hook/adapter/settings drift before a ratified gate is constrained by the future adapter contract (which records the subordination clause and the canonical adapter behaviors); the Security/Trust portion (hook activation, hook drift, settings drift relative to the ratified hook-activation discipline) remains coupled to a separately approved `R-2` ratification. Final disposition of `P02-RISK-007` therefore remains coupled to a separately approved `R-2` ratification gate in addition to a separately approved Product Owner risk-disposition gate. This decision does not mutate `governance/RISK_REGISTER.md`.
  - The **reinforced-for-Agent-Adapter-only** posture for `P02-ROAD-001` is that the Agent-Adapter dependency surface of "Resolve Domain-Model Open Questions" proceeds against the future separately ratified adapter contract document as the canonical realization surface; the Domain-dimension bound already established by `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-002` and reinforced by `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-002` (canonical realization surface is the future thin structured projection under Option `D-B`) remains unchanged and is not modified by this decision; the Governance-Code dimension portion remains coupled to any separately approved `R-5`-related follow-up. Final scheduling of `P02-ROAD-001` remains a separately approved Product Owner roadmap-scheduling gate. This decision does not mutate `governance/ROADMAP.md`.
  - No code, runtime, hook, settings, adapter-rule, dependency, license, or runtime context pack is authorized to act on this Agent-Adapter Boundary posture at this time. Implementation remains gated by P04 GO. Project code remains separate from governance and requires later explicit implementation authorization. The current Claude Code adapter surface (`CLAUDE.md`, `AGENTS.md`, `.claude/rules/**`, `.claude/skills/**`, `.claude/agents/**`, `.claude/hooks/**`, `.claude/settings.json`, `.claude/settings.local.example.json`) is **not** modified, retroactively reframed, or elevated by this decision; it remains subordinate behavioral guidance until the future adapter contract is separately ratified.

## DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-004

- decision_id: `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-004`
- status: `RATIFIED`
- decision: Canonicalize P03 architecture decision record `ADR-DRAFT-P03-006` (**Agent-Adapter Boundary**) from `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_EVALUATION_PACKAGE.md` §7 as the canonical Agent-Adapter Boundary ADR under `CONT-P03-ARCH-001`, consistent with already-ratified `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-004` and preserving the selected Agent-Adapter Boundary option `A-C` (adapter abstraction via a future `ADAPTER_CONTRACT.md`-like artifact). Canonical ADR content (verbatim from §7): "ADR-DRAFT-P03-006 — Agent-Adapter Boundary. context: `Agent-1..8` plus existing `CLAUDE.md` / `.claude/rules/**` define adapter behavior; only one adapter exists today. decision (proposed): adopt Option A-C (adapter abstraction via a future `ADAPTER_CONTRACT.md`-like artifact), staged from the current Option A-A single-adapter state (Recommendation R-6). consequences (proposed): governance remains single-sourced; adapter rules remain subordinate behavioral guidance; multi-adapter expansion possible without ad-hoc divergence; first adopter remains Claude Code. alternatives considered: Option A-A (single adapter indefinitely); Option A-B (multi-adapter without a formal contract)." Under this ratification the ADR's content moves from `status: proposed` (in the package) to canonical ADR status as a `governance/DECISION_LOG.md` row under the `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-NNN` family; alternative options `A-A` (single adapter indefinitely — current trajectory carried forward without contract abstraction) and `A-B` (multi-adapter with shared governance but without a formal contract) are not adopted as the canonical posture; per `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-004`, Option `A-A` continues as the *interim* surface only until a formal `ADAPTER_CONTRACT.md`-like artifact is separately ratified under a separately approved Product Owner gate, and Option `A-B` is not adopted at any horizon under this decision. This decision is the fourth row in the `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-NNN` family, sequenced after `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-002`, and `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-003`. This ADR ratification canonicalizes the already-ratified `R-6` posture (under `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-004`) as an ADR decision; it does not re-ratify `R-6` as a recommendation.

- decision_family: `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-NNN` (per `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_RATIFICATION_PLAN.md` §9). This decision is the fourth row in the `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-NNN` family, sequenced after `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-002`, and `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-003`.
- related_prior_decisions: `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-004`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-003`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-003`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-002`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-002`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-004`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-003`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-002`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001`, `DEC-P03-ACTIVATION-001`.

  - `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-004` (which ratified `R-6` with Option `A-C`, adapter abstraction via a future `ADAPTER_CONTRACT.md`-like artifact) remains canonical and unchanged. `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-004` canonicalizes the ADR-form expression of the same Agent-Adapter Boundary posture without altering, re-ratifying, modifying, or superseding `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-004`. The canonical Agent-Adapter Boundary Architecture remains Option `A-C`; the future separately ratified vendor-neutral adapter contract document (e.g. `ADAPTER_CONTRACT.md`) is the canonical realization surface (defining required adapter behaviors — cold-start reading, authority order, approval-verb discipline, never-automatic surface — with each vendor adapter implementing the contract while governance remains single-sourced); the current Claude Code adapter surface remains the only adapter surface today (Option `A-A` interim state) until that contract is introduced under a separately approved Product Owner gate — exactly as ratified under `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-004`.
  - `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-001` (which ratified `R-5` with Option `B-B`, governance-as-contract) and `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-001` (which canonicalized `ADR-DRAFT-P03-005` with the same Option `B-B` posture) remain canonical and unchanged. The canonical-wins discipline of `B-B` (governance-as-contract) is preserved here at the ADR level for the Agent-Adapter Boundary dimension: the future vendor-neutral adapter contract is itself a governance document subject to the same canonical-wins discipline, and any future derived adapter artifact (per-vendor adapter file, projection, or similar) is subordinate and never elevated to authority.
  - `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-002` (which ratified `R-1` with Option `D-B`, governance-first with thin structured projection) and `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-002` (which canonicalized `ADR-DRAFT-P03-001` with the same Option `D-B` posture) remain canonical and unchanged. The governance-first authority surface of `D-B` is preserved here at the ADR level for the Agent-Adapter Boundary dimension: the future vendor-neutral adapter contract is a governance-first authority surface — a separately ratified governance document — and any future derived projection of agent identity, agent behavior, or adapter mapping remains subordinate and never elevated to authority.
  - `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-003` (which ratified `R-3` with Option `C-C`, dedicated classification registry) and `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-003` (which canonicalized `ADR-DRAFT-P03-003` with the same Option `C-C` posture) remain canonical and unchanged. The dedicated-governance-document realization pattern of `C-C` is preserved here at the ADR level for the Agent-Adapter Boundary dimension: both posture choices share the same pattern — a separately ratified governance document (classification registry for `R-3`/`ADR-003`; adapter contract for `R-6`/`ADR-006`) records canonical content and existing per-document or per-adapter surfaces remain unchanged until that separately ratified document is introduced under its own Product Owner gate.
  - This decision does not re-ratify `R-6`, `R-1`, `R-3`, `R-5`, `ADR-DRAFT-P03-001`, `ADR-DRAFT-P03-003`, or `ADR-DRAFT-P03-005`, and does not modify or supersede `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-002`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-003`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-004`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-002`, or `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-003`.
- safety_basis:
  - `ADR-DRAFT-P03-006` shares the architecture content of `R-6` and therefore shares the same directly-conditioning `P03-blocking` dependency surface under the ratified G-4 classification `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001`: two `P03-blocking` `OQ-P02-*` rows, one `P03-blocking` `P02-RISK-*` row, and two `P03-blocking` `P02-ROAD-*` rows in the Agent-Adapter Boundary dimension — `OQ-P02-D-007` (`Agent` as domain concept vs adapter/runtime concern), `OQ-P02-S-005` (Agent-behavior split between governance and adapter rules), `P02-RISK-007` (Hook / Adapter / Settings Drift Before Ratified Gate — **cross-coupled with `R-2`**), `P02-ROAD-001` (Resolve Domain-Model Open Questions — **cross-coupled across Domain / Governance-Code / Agent-Adapter dimensions**), and `P02-ROAD-009` (Decide Adapter-Rule vs Governance Split for Agent Behavior). Per `governance/P03_G4_CLASSIFICATION_PLAN.md` §5/§6/§7 these rows are classified `P03-blocking` because each "directly conditions R-6 / ADR-DRAFT-P03-006 (Agent-Adapter Boundary)" (or, for `P02-ROAD-009`, "drives R-6 / ADR-DRAFT-P03-006 (Agent-Adapter Boundary)"; for `P02-RISK-007`, "Directly affects R-2 / ADR-DRAFT-P03-002 staging and R-6 / ADR-DRAFT-P03-006 adapter-rule subordination"; for `P02-ROAD-001`, "Scheduling aligned with R-1 / R-5 / R-6 ratifications").
  - `OQ-P02-D-007`, `OQ-P02-S-005`, and `P02-ROAD-009` are already architecture-posture-**bounded** by `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-004` (canonical realization surface is the future separately ratified vendor-neutral adapter contract document). Canonicalizing `ADR-DRAFT-P03-006` under `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-004` **reinforces** the same architecture-posture bound at the ADR level — the canonical Agent-Adapter Boundary ADR records the same adapter-abstraction-via-future-contract posture — without resolving the per-row semantic content of those rows (the specific agent contract clauses, the specific behavior split, the specific roadmap scheduling) and without mutating any of those rows in `governance/OPEN_QUESTIONS.md` or `governance/ROADMAP.md`. Final per-row disposition of `OQ-P02-D-007`, final per-row disposition of `OQ-P02-S-005`, and final per-row scheduling of `P02-ROAD-009` each remain separately approved Product Owner gates and are not performed by this decision.
  - `P02-RISK-007` (Hook / Adapter / Settings Drift Before Ratified Gate) is only **partially** architecture-posture-reinforced-bounded by this ADR ratification for the Agent-Adapter Boundary dimension. Per `governance/P03_G4_CLASSIFICATION_PLAN.md` §6 the row's resolution is "Resolved jointly with R-2 / R-6 ratifications" — it is **cross-coupled** between the Security/Trust dimension (`R-2`) and the Agent-Adapter Boundary dimension (`R-6`). Already partially bounded by `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-004` for the Agent-Adapter Boundary dimension only; `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-004` reinforces the Agent-Adapter Boundary portion of that bound at the ADR level (the canonical adapter-rule and settings surface for the future adapter contract will be the contract itself plus the subordination clause it records; vendor adapters remain subordinate behavioral guidance; adapter rules and settings remain non-authoritative against governance). The Security/Trust validation portion of `P02-RISK-007` (hook activation, hook drift, settings drift relative to the ratified hook-activation discipline) is **not** bounded by this ADR ratification; final disposition of `P02-RISK-007` remains coupled to a separately approved `R-2` revision/ratification gate and a separate Product Owner risk-register follow-up gate. The row is not mutated in `governance/RISK_REGISTER.md` by this decision.
  - `P02-ROAD-001` (Resolve Domain-Model Open Questions) is already architecture-posture-**bounded** by `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-002` and reinforced at ADR level by `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-002` for the Domain dimension under Option `D-B`, and architecture-posture-**reinforced-for-Agent-Adapter-only** by `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-004` for the Agent-Adapter Boundary dependency surface. Per `governance/P03_G4_CLASSIFICATION_PLAN.md` §7 the row's dimension is "Cross-cutting (Domain + Governance-Code + Agent-Adapter)" and its scheduling is "Scheduling aligned with R-1 / R-5 / R-6 ratifications". `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-004` **reinforces at ADR level** the Agent-Adapter Boundary dependency surface portion of that bound only — the canonical realization surface for the Agent-Adapter portion of `P02-ROAD-001`'s scheduling is the future separately ratified adapter contract document — without modifying the Domain-dimension bound already established by `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-002` and reinforced by `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-002` and without addressing the Governance-Code dimension (which remains coupled to any separately approved `R-5`-related follow-up if any). This decision does not mutate `governance/ROADMAP.md`; final scheduling of `P02-ROAD-001` remains a separately approved Product Owner roadmap-scheduling gate.
  - Structural cross-cutting `P03-blocking` risks `P02-RISK-001`, `P02-RISK-002`, `P02-RISK-005`, `P02-RISK-006`, and `P02-RISK-018` are reaffirmed without mutation; ratifying `ADR-DRAFT-P03-006` at the canonical-Agent-Adapter-Boundary-ADR surface is consistent with those structural risks remaining canonically open in `governance/RISK_REGISTER.md` until separately disposed.
  - The decision aligns with ratified `governance/CONTEXT_POLICY.md` canonical-wins discipline (P-4), ratified `governance/TRUST_BOUNDARIES.md` Mutation / Scope-Bound boundary rules, and the canonical-authority-surface discipline of `governance/TRUST_BOUNDARIES.md`.
  - `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-004` satisfies `I-1` (per `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-001`): it is recorded as its own distinct row in `governance/DECISION_LOG.md`, separate from `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-004`.
  - `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-004` satisfies `I-2` (per `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-004`): it is the canonical ADR row for `ADR-DRAFT-P03-006`, recorded under the `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-NNN` family in its final canonical form.
  - `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-004` satisfies `I-7` (per `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-002`): the `non_authorizations:` section below explicitly enumerates what this decision does not authorize.
  - `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-004` preserves `I-8` (per `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-003`): it does not open P03 closeout and does not open P04 GO; both require separately approved Product Owner gates.
- bounded_rows:
  - `OQ-P02-D-007` — architecture-posture-bounded (canonical realization surface is the future separately ratified vendor-neutral adapter contract document; `Agent` as domain concept vs adapter/runtime concern is canonically resolved inside that contract document — agent identity, agent authority order, agent approval-verb discipline, and agent never-automatic surface are recorded as contract terms — under its own separately approved Product Owner gate). Already bounded by `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-004`; reinforced at ADR level by `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-004`. Source register `governance/OPEN_QUESTIONS.md` remains unchanged. The roadmap row remains `Proposed; not started` until a separately approved Product Owner roadmap-scheduling gate.
- forward_application:
  - The canonical Agent-Adapter Boundary Architecture is Option `A-C` (adapter abstraction via a future `ADAPTER_CONTRACT.md`-like artifact), now recorded at both recommendation level (`DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-004`) and ADR level (`DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-004`).
  - Any future ratified generator, validator, or projection from the vendor-neutral adapter contract artifact (registry-derived check, projection artifact, automated mapping consumer, per-vendor adapter implementation, or similar) must be authorized by a separately approved Product Owner gate, and the artifact must remain subordinate and never elevated to authority.
  - Creation, generation, population, and registration of the future vendor-neutral adapter contract document itself remain separately approved Product Owner gates that must explicitly define the canonical required adapter behaviors (cold-start reading, authority order, approval-verb discipline, never-automatic surface), the agent-identity / agent-authority-order / agent-approval-verb / agent-never-automatic-surface content, the subordination clause, and the document-registry registration.
  - Creation, registration, or activation of any additional vendor adapter (e.g. an `AGENTS.md`-anchored second-adapter surface) remains separately gated on (a) the prior ratification of the future vendor-neutral adapter contract document and (b) a separately approved Product Owner gate for adding the second adapter under that contract.
  - Any future ADR revision affecting `ADR-DRAFT-P03-006` requires a `DEC-P03-ARCH-REVISION-NNN` decision and must remain consistent with `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-004` (or be paired with explicit supersession/revision of `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-004`).

## DEC-P03-ARCH-REVISION-001

- decision_id: `DEC-P03-ARCH-REVISION-001`
- status: `RATIFIED`
- decision: Ratify the **Step D source-package revision** of the `R-2` recommendation and the `ADR-DRAFT-P03-002` ADR draft in `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_EVALUATION_PACKAGE.md` §6 / §7 — adding explicit S-A → S-B → (post-P04) S-C staging vocabulary and an explicit staged-posture-to-trust-boundary mapping (Authority boundary, Mutation boundary, Evidence boundary, Context boundary, Secret / Identity boundary, Agent / Adapter boundary, Misuse / never-automatic surface) per `DEC-P02-SECURITY-TRUST-REQUIREMENTS-001` candidate vocabulary (`Authority-1..7` / `Mutation-1..8` / `Evidence-1..6` / `Context-1..6` / `Secret-1..6` / `Agent-1..8` / `Misuse-1..12`) and identity discipline (`Identity-Bound-1..3` per `governance/TRUST_BOUNDARIES.md`); marking each S-stage as a separately approved Product Owner gate (Option `S-B` hook activation = source-package Gate G-5, not authorized here; Option `S-C` layered enforcement remains post-P04, not authorized here); and explicitly noting that the revised `R-2` and `ADR-DRAFT-P03-002` material remain `status: proposed` in the package until separately ratified under the `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-NNN` family (`R-2`) and the `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-NNN` family (`ADR-DRAFT-P03-002`) per `I-2` (`DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-004`). This decision is the **first row in the `DEC-P03-ARCH-REVISION-NNN` family**. It ratifies **only the source-package revision** of the `R-2` / `ADR-DRAFT-P03-002` material per Step D of `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_RATIFICATION_PLAN.md` §6; it modifies **only the proposed source-package text**, not any canonical ratified architecture posture. `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_EVALUATION_PACKAGE.md` remains `PROPOSED_INACTIVE` / `NOT_RATIFIED`; the revision does not elevate the document's status. `R-2` is **still not ratified** (recommendation remains `status: proposed`; ratification requires a separately approved Product Owner gate under the `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-NNN` family). `ADR-DRAFT-P03-002` is **still not ratified** (ADR draft remains `status: proposed`; ratification requires a separately approved Product Owner gate under the `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-NNN` family per `I-2`, and only after the underlying `R-2` recommendation is separately ratified). The revision makes `R-2` **eligible** for a later separate Product Owner recommendation ratification under `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-NNN`, if the Product Owner selects it; and makes `ADR-DRAFT-P03-002` **eligible** for a later separate Product Owner ADR ratification under `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-NNN` only after `R-2` is later ratified, preserving `I-2`.

## DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-005

- decision_id: `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-005`
- status: `RATIFIED`
- decision: Ratify P03 architecture recommendation `R-2` (**Security / Trust**) from `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_EVALUATION_PACKAGE.md` §6 with the **staged Security / Trust posture** (Option `S-A` → Option `S-B` → (post-P04) Option `S-C`) as revised under `DEC-P03-ARCH-REVISION-001` and using the revised package wording verbatim. The recommended path is **staged, not immediate enforcement**: stage from Option `S-A` (advisory-only documentation, current trajectory) to Option `S-B` (advisory + separately approved hooks/checks, gated by `54 pass / 0 fail` fixture evidence and explicit Product Owner activation per `governance/CHANGE_PROTOCOL.md` and `governance/NEVER_AUTOMATIC.md`) to (post-P04) Option `S-C` (layered enforcement after later gates). The staged posture is mapped to the trust-boundary surfaces per ratified `governance/P02_SECURITY_TRUST_REQUIREMENTS_DRAFT.md` candidate vocabulary (`Authority-1..7` / `Mutation-1..8` / `Evidence-1..6` / `Context-1..6` / `Secret-1..6` / `Agent-1..8` / `Misuse-1..12`) and ratified `governance/TRUST_BOUNDARIES.md` identity discipline (`Identity-Bound-1..3`): **Authority boundary** — `S-A`: `Authority-1..7` advisory in governance/adapter rules (Product Owner sole ratification, approval-verb discipline); `S-B`: selected `Authority-1..7` additionally enforced by separately approved Product-Owner-activated hooks/checks (no hook activated by this ratification); `S-C`: post-P04 layered enforcement (not authorized by this ratification). **Mutation boundary** — `S-A`: `Mutation-1..8` advisory (file-allowlist discipline, no destructive Git without approval, no unscoped writes); `S-B`: selected `Mutation-1..8` additionally enforced by separately approved hooks (e.g. file-scope check, destructive-command guard) under hook-activation discipline (no hook activated by this ratification); `S-C`: post-P04 layered enforcement (not authorized by this ratification). **Evidence boundary** — `S-A`: `Evidence-1..6` advisory (durable evidence in task records, fixture results, validation evidence); `S-B`: selected `Evidence-1..6` additionally enforced by separately approved validation hooks/checks under hook-activation discipline (no hook, validator, or automated check activated by this ratification); `S-C`: post-P04 layered enforcement (not authorized by this ratification). **Context boundary** — `S-A`: `Context-1..6` advisory (canonical-wins, subordination of derived/generated context, cold-start reading discipline, no automatic context elevation); `S-B`: selected `Context-1..6` additionally enforced by separately approved freshness/staleness checks under hook-activation discipline (no hook activated by this ratification); `S-C`: post-P04 layered enforcement (not authorized by this ratification). Independent of `R-4` / `ADR-DRAFT-P03-004` runtime-context-pack acceptance criteria, which are pending Step E revision under a separate `DEC-P03-ARCH-REVISION-NNN` gate (not this ratification); no runtime context pack generation is authorized by this ratification. **Secret / Identity boundary** — `S-A`: `Secret-1..6` and `Identity-Bound-1..3` advisory (`.env` / `.env.*` / `.claude/settings.local.json` / `CLAUDE.local.md` / `secrets/**` never read; no secret values in repo/logs/governance; `Rauf Alizada` sole Product Owner; `Raauf Alizada` invalid; `Tural Rahmanli` not a project identity); `S-B`: selected `Secret-1..6` / `Identity-Bound-1..3` additionally enforced by separately approved hooks (e.g. secret-file read prevention, identity-string checker) under hook-activation discipline (no hook activated by this ratification); `S-C`: post-P04 layered enforcement (not authorized by this ratification). **Agent / Adapter boundary** — `S-A`: `Agent-1..8` advisory (cold-start reading, authority order, approval-verb discipline, never-automatic surface, agent behavior split per already-ratified `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-004` / `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-004` under Option `A-C` adapter abstraction via a future `ADAPTER_CONTRACT.md`-like artifact); `S-B`: selected `Agent-1..8` additionally enforced by separately approved hooks (e.g. approval-verb guard) under hook-activation discipline (no hook activated by this ratification); `S-C`: post-P04 layered enforcement (not authorized by this ratification). The canonical realization surface for `Agent-1..8` content remains the future separately ratified vendor-neutral adapter contract document under Option `A-C` (subordination preserved; never elevated to authority). **Misuse / never-automatic surface** — `S-A`: `Misuse-1..12` advisory (no auto-actions outside ratified gates per `governance/NEVER_AUTOMATIC.md`; the never-automatic surface is preserved structurally); `S-B`: selected `Misuse-1..12` additionally enforced by separately approved hooks (e.g. never-automatic guard) under hook-activation discipline (no hook activated by this ratification); `S-C`: post-P04 layered enforcement (not authorized by this ratification). Does **not** modify or supersede `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-001..004`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-001..004`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-001..004`, or `DEC-P03-ARCH-REVISION-001`. Does **not** modify `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_RATIFICATION_PLAN.md` or `governance/P03_G4_CLASSIFICATION_PLAN.md`. Does **not** elevate the status of `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_EVALUATION_PACKAGE.md`. Does **not** mutate any source register (`OQ-P02-S-001`, `OQ-P02-S-009`, `OQ-P02-C-009`, `P02-RISK-007` Security/Trust-leg-bounded but not mutated; cross-coupled Data-Classification / Agent-Adapter legs remain under their respective partial-bound decisions; `OQ-P02-D-001`, `OQ-P02-D-007`, `OQ-P02-D-008`, `OQ-P02-S-005`, `OQ-P02-C-001`, `OQ-P02-C-010`, `P02-RISK-016`, `P02-RISK-017`, `P02-ROAD-001`, `P02-ROAD-002`, `P02-ROAD-009` not affected by this decision). Does **not** authorize hook activation (Option `S-B` Gate G-5 remains separately approved), Option `S-C` layered enforcement, settings changes, adapter-rule changes, validator/automated-check activation, enforcement, implementation, project code, dependencies, license, runtime context pack generation, adapter-contract artifact creation, classification-registry file creation, adapter implementation, connector code, or security enforcement controls. Does **not** create any P04 or P05 task; does **not** open P03 closeout; does **not** open P04 GO. Subsequent per-ADR (`ADR-DRAFT-P03-002`), per-criterion, per-row, P03-closeout, and P04-activation ratification gates remain separately required.

## DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-005

- decision_id: `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-005`
- status: `RATIFIED`
- decision: Canonicalize P03 architecture decision record `ADR-DRAFT-P03-002` (**Security/Trust Enforcement Path**) from `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_EVALUATION_PACKAGE.md` §7 as the canonical Security/Trust Enforcement Path ADR under `CONT-P03-ARCH-001`, consistent with already-ratified `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-005` and preserving the selected staged Security / Trust posture (Option `S-A` advisory-only documentation, current trajectory → Option `S-B` advisory + separately approved hooks/checks → Option `S-C` post-P04 layered enforcement) per Recommendation `R-2` and using verbatim the Step D-revised package wording ratified under `DEC-P03-ARCH-REVISION-001`. Canonical ADR content (verbatim from §7): "ADR-DRAFT-P03-002 — Security/Trust Enforcement Path. context: `DEC-P02-SECURITY-TRUST-REQUIREMENTS-001` surfaces candidate `Authority-1..7` / `Mutation-1..8` / `Evidence-1..6` / `Context-1..6` / `Secret-1..6` / `Agent-1..8` / `Misuse-1..12` requirements and `governance/TRUST_BOUNDARIES.md` records `Identity-Bound-1..3`; hooks remain advisory. The existing Claude Code adapter surface (`CLAUDE.md`, `AGENTS.md`, `.claude/rules/**`, `.claude/skills/**`, `.claude/agents/**`, `.claude/hooks/**`, `.claude/settings.json`, `.claude/settings.local.example.json`) is the only adapter surface today; the future vendor-neutral adapter contract document under Option `A-C` (already-ratified `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-004` / `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-004`) is the canonical realization surface for `Agent-1..8` content. decision (proposed): stage Option `S-A` (advisory-only documentation, current trajectory) → Option `S-B` (advisory + separately approved hooks/checks) → Option `S-C` (post-P04 layered enforcement) per Recommendation `R-2`, with the explicit staged-posture-to-trust-boundary mapping recorded in §6 (R-2) — **Authority boundary**, **Mutation boundary**, **Evidence boundary**, **Context boundary**, **Secret / Identity boundary**, **Agent / Adapter boundary**, **Misuse / never-automatic surface** — and with each stage requiring its own separately approved Product Owner gate: Option `S-B` hook activation gated by `54 pass / 0 fail` fixture evidence and explicit Product Owner activation per `governance/CHANGE_PROTOCOL.md` and `governance/NEVER_AUTOMATIC.md` (source-package Gate G-5; **not authorized by this revision**); Option `S-C` layered enforcement remains post-P04 and requires its own separately approved Product Owner gate (**not authorized by this revision**). consequences (proposed): codifies the advisory baseline (`S-A`) as the current canonical posture without ratifying it here; clears a **staged** path to activated hooks under existing discipline (`S-B`) without authorizing hook activation; preserves honest layering ('no single layer is complete isolation'); aligns with `Identity-Bound-1..3` identity discipline (`Rauf Alizada` sole Product Owner; `Raauf Alizada` invalid; `Tural Rahmanli` not a project identity) and the never-automatic surface (`governance/NEVER_AUTOMATIC.md`); consistent with already-ratified `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-001..004` and `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-001..004` (Options `B-B`, `D-B`, `C-C`, `A-C`); the future vendor-neutral adapter contract under Option `A-C` is the canonical realization surface for `Agent-1..8` content (subordination preserved; never elevated to authority); canonical-wins discipline preserved; `I-8` preserved (no P03 closeout opened; no P04 GO opened); no `.claude/hooks/**`, `.claude/settings.json`, `.claude/settings.local.example.json`, `CLAUDE.md`, `AGENTS.md`, `.claude/rules/**`, `.claude/skills/**`, `.claude/agents/**`, dependencies, lockfiles, manifests, license, project code, runtime context packs, or vendor-neutral adapter contract artifacts are modified or authorized by this ADR draft or by `DEC-P03-ARCH-REVISION-001`. alternatives considered: stay on Option `S-A` indefinitely (advisory-only, no path to activated hooks; rejected because it leaves `Authority-1..7` / `Mutation-1..8` / `Evidence-1..6` / `Context-1..6` / `Secret-1..6` / `Agent-1..8` / `Misuse-1..12` unmappable to any later technical control surface); jump straight to Option `S-C` without staged activation (rejected because it violates layered-not-absolute representation, the ratified hook-activation discipline, and the `54 pass / 0 fail` fixture-evidence prerequisite); skip Option `S-B` and stage `S-A → S-C` directly (rejected for the same hook-activation-discipline reasons because `S-C` presupposes layered enforcement on top of `S-B`)." Under this ratification the ADR's content moves from `status: proposed` (in the package, Step D-revised under `DEC-P03-ARCH-REVISION-001`) to canonical ADR status as a `governance/DECISION_LOG.md` row under the `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-NNN` family; alternative postures (remain indefinitely on Option `S-A` with no path to Option `S-B`; jump directly to Option `S-C` without staged activation; skip Option `S-B` and stage `S-A → S-C` directly) are not adopted as the canonical posture, exactly as ratified under `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-005`. This decision is the fifth row in the `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-NNN` family, sequenced after `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-002`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-003`, and `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-004`. This ADR ratification canonicalizes the already-ratified `R-2` posture (under `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-005`) as an ADR decision; it does not re-ratify `R-2` as a recommendation.

  - `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-005` (which ratified `R-2` with the staged Security / Trust posture `S-A` → `S-B` → (post-P04) `S-C` using verbatim the Step D-revised package wording ratified under `DEC-P03-ARCH-REVISION-001`) remains canonical and unchanged. `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-005` canonicalizes the ADR-form expression of the same Security / Trust Enforcement Path posture without altering, re-ratifying, modifying, or superseding `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-005`. The canonical Security / Trust architecture posture remains the staged `S-A` → `S-B` → (post-P04) `S-C` path with the explicit per-trust-boundary mapping across **Authority boundary**, **Mutation boundary**, **Evidence boundary**, **Context boundary**, **Secret / Identity boundary**, **Agent / Adapter boundary**, and **Misuse / never-automatic surface** per ratified `governance/P02_SECURITY_TRUST_REQUIREMENTS_DRAFT.md` candidate vocabulary (`Authority-1..7` / `Mutation-1..8` / `Evidence-1..6` / `Context-1..6` / `Secret-1..6` / `Agent-1..8` / `Misuse-1..12`) and ratified `governance/TRUST_BOUNDARIES.md` identity discipline (`Identity-Bound-1..3`); Option `S-A` (advisory-only documentation) is the current canonical baseline; Option `S-B` (advisory + separately approved hooks/checks) remains source-package Gate G-5 (separately approved Product Owner gate per `governance/CHANGE_PROTOCOL.md` and `governance/NEVER_AUTOMATIC.md`; `54 pass / 0 fail` fixture-evidence prerequisite; **not authorized** by this ADR ratification); Option `S-C` (post-P04 layered enforcement) requires its own separately approved Product Owner gate (**not authorized** by this ADR ratification) — exactly as ratified under `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-005`.

- safety_basis:
  - `ADR-DRAFT-P03-002` shares the architecture content of `R-2` and therefore shares the same directly-conditioning `P03-blocking` dependency surface under the ratified G-4 classification `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001`: two `P03-blocking` `OQ-P02-S-*` rows directly in the Security / Trust dimension and two cross-coupled `P03-blocking` rows — `OQ-P02-S-001` (Which candidate security/trust requirements become canonical vs deferred), `OQ-P02-S-009` (Governance-level validation before hook activation), `OQ-P02-C-009` (governance-level validation of handling requirements — **cross-coupled with `R-3`**), and `P02-RISK-007` (Hook / Adapter / Settings Drift Before Ratified Gate — **cross-coupled with `R-6`**). Per `governance/P03_G4_CLASSIFICATION_PLAN.md` §5/§6 these rows are classified `P03-blocking` because each "directly conditions R-2 / ADR-DRAFT-P03-002 (Security/Trust)" (or, for `OQ-P02-C-009`, "Resolved jointly with R-2 / R-3 revisions and ratifications"; for `P02-RISK-007`, "Directly affects R-2 / ADR-DRAFT-P03-002 staging and R-6 / ADR-DRAFT-P03-006 adapter-rule subordination").
  - `OQ-P02-S-001` and `OQ-P02-S-009` are already architecture-posture-**bounded** for the Security / Trust dimension by `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-005`. Canonicalizing `ADR-DRAFT-P03-002` under `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-005` **reinforces** the same architecture-posture bound at the ADR level — the canonical Security / Trust Enforcement Path ADR records the same staged `S-A` → `S-B` → (post-P04) `S-C` posture with the explicit per-trust-boundary mapping — without resolving the per-row semantic content of those rows (the specific canonical-vs-deferred selection for the candidate security/trust requirements; the specific governance-level validation requirements before hook activation) and without mutating any of those rows in `governance/OPEN_QUESTIONS.md`. Final per-row disposition of `OQ-P02-S-001` and `OQ-P02-S-009` each remain separately approved Product Owner gates and are not performed by this decision.
  - `OQ-P02-C-009` (governance-level validation of handling requirements) is already architecture-posture-**partially bounded** for the Data Classification dimension by `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-003` / `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-003` and architecture-posture-bounded for the Security / Trust dimension by `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-005`. `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-005` **reinforces** the Security / Trust dimension portion of that bound at the ADR level — the canonical Security / Trust Enforcement Path ADR records the same staged posture for the Security / Trust leg — without modifying the Data Classification dimension bound already established by `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-003` and reinforced by `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-003`. The row is not mutated in `governance/OPEN_QUESTIONS.md` by this decision; final per-row disposition of `OQ-P02-C-009` remains coupled to a separate Product Owner open-questions follow-up gate.
  - `P02-RISK-007` (Hook / Adapter / Settings Drift Before Ratified Gate) is already architecture-posture-**partially bounded** for the Agent-Adapter Boundary dimension by `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-004` / `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-004` and architecture-posture-bounded for the Security / Trust dimension by `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-005`. Per `governance/P03_G4_CLASSIFICATION_PLAN.md` §6 the row's resolution is "Resolved jointly with R-2 / R-6 ratifications" — it is **cross-coupled** between the Security / Trust dimension (`R-2`) and the Agent-Adapter Boundary dimension (`R-6`). `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-005` **reinforces** the Security / Trust dimension portion of that bound at the ADR level — the canonical Security / Trust Enforcement Path ADR records the same staged posture for the Security / Trust leg, including the explicit subordination of any future hook/adapter/settings technical-control surface to governance and the explicit hook-activation discipline (Option `S-B` Gate G-5 prerequisite; Option `S-C` post-P04 gate prerequisite) — without modifying the Agent-Adapter Boundary dimension bound already established by `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-004` and reinforced by `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-004`. The row is not mutated in `governance/RISK_REGISTER.md` by this decision; final disposition of `P02-RISK-007` remains a separately approved Product Owner risk-register follow-up gate.
  - Structural cross-cutting `P03-blocking` risks `P02-RISK-001`, `P02-RISK-002`, `P02-RISK-005`, `P02-RISK-006`, and `P02-RISK-018` are reaffirmed without mutation; canonicalizing `ADR-DRAFT-P03-002` at the canonical-Security/Trust-Enforcement-Path-ADR surface is consistent with those structural risks remaining canonically open in `governance/RISK_REGISTER.md` until separately disposed.
  - The decision aligns with ratified `governance/CONTEXT_POLICY.md` canonical-wins discipline (P-4), ratified `governance/TRUST_BOUNDARIES.md` Mutation / Scope-Bound / Identity-Bound boundary rules, the candidate-vs-canonical pattern established in `DEC-P02-SECURITY-TRUST-REQUIREMENTS-001`, and the canonical-authority-surface discipline of `governance/TRUST_BOUNDARIES.md`. The staged-not-immediate-enforcement posture preserves the ratified hook-activation discipline (`governance/CHANGE_PROTOCOL.md` / `governance/NEVER_AUTOMATIC.md`) and the layered-not-absolute representation (no single layer is represented as complete isolation).
  - `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-005` satisfies `I-1` (per `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-001`): it is recorded as its own distinct row in `governance/DECISION_LOG.md`, separate from `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-005` and from any other decision row.
  - `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-005` satisfies `I-2` (per `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-004`): it is the canonical ADR row for `ADR-DRAFT-P03-002`, recorded under the `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-NNN` family in its final canonical form. The underlying `R-2` recommendation prerequisite is satisfied by `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-005`.
  - `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-005` satisfies `I-7` (per `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-002`): the `non_authorizations:` section below explicitly enumerates what this decision does not authorize.
  - `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-005` preserves `I-8` (per `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-003`): it does not open P03 closeout and does not open P04 GO; both require separately approved Product Owner gates.

- forward_application:
  - The canonical Security / Trust Enforcement Path Architecture is the staged `S-A` → `S-B` → (post-P04) `S-C` path with the explicit per-trust-boundary mapping across **Authority boundary**, **Mutation boundary**, **Evidence boundary**, **Context boundary**, **Secret / Identity boundary**, **Agent / Adapter boundary**, and **Misuse / never-automatic surface**, now recorded at both recommendation level (`DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-005`) and ADR level (`DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-005`).
  - Any future ratified hook, validator, automated check, settings entry, or adapter-rule projection arising from Option `S-B` of the canonical staged Security / Trust posture must be authorized by a separately approved Product Owner Gate G-5 (or later Product Owner gate), must satisfy the `54 pass / 0 fail` fixture-evidence prerequisite per `governance/CHANGE_PROTOCOL.md` and `governance/NEVER_AUTOMATIC.md`, and must remain subordinate and never elevated to authority.
  - Any future ratified Option `S-C` (post-P04 layered enforcement) advancement requires its own separately approved Product Owner gate after P04 GO and remains a separate gate.
  - Creation, registration, or activation of any hook, validator, automated check, settings change, adapter-rule change, adapter-contract artifact, classification-registry artifact, adapter implementation, connector code, or security enforcement control remains a separately approved Product Owner gate that must explicitly define the canonical required behaviors, scope, evidence prerequisite, document-registry implications, and subordination clause.
  - Any future ADR revision affecting `ADR-DRAFT-P03-002` requires a `DEC-P03-ARCH-REVISION-NNN` decision (numbering monotonic, starting from `002` for the next revision row) and must remain consistent with `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-005` (or be paired with explicit supersession/revision of `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-005`).

## DEC-P03-ARCH-REVISION-002

- decision_id: `DEC-P03-ARCH-REVISION-002`
- status: `RATIFIED`
- decision: Ratify the **Step E source-package revision** of the `R-4` recommendation and the `ADR-DRAFT-P03-004` ADR draft in `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_EVALUATION_PACKAGE.md` §6 / §7 — adding an enumerated, explicit eight-item runtime-context-pack acceptance-criteria set (generator provenance, freshness check, staleness halt evidence, subordination clause, hard token cap, observable generation, reversibility, explicit non-elevation) per `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_RATIFICATION_PLAN.md` §6 and §7 E-7; mapping the eight criteria to the `P03-blocking` source-register rows `OQ-P02-D-005`, `OQ-P02-C-004`, `P02-RISK-003`, `P02-RISK-004`, and `P02-ROAD-006` per `governance/P03_G4_CLASSIFICATION_PLAN.md`; and explicitly stating that runtime context pack generation is **not authorized** by this revision under any condition (generation itself remains source-package Gate G-6, a separately approved future Product Owner gate). This decision is the **second row** in the `DEC-P03-ARCH-REVISION-NNN` family, following `DEC-P03-ARCH-REVISION-001` (Step D, `R-2` / `ADR-DRAFT-P03-002`). It ratifies **only the source-package revision** of the `R-4` / `ADR-DRAFT-P03-004` material per Step E of `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_RATIFICATION_PLAN.md` §6; it modifies **only the proposed source-package text**, not any canonical ratified architecture posture. `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_EVALUATION_PACKAGE.md` remains `PROPOSED_INACTIVE` / `NOT_RATIFIED`; the revision does not elevate the document's status. `R-4` is **still not ratified** (recommendation remains `status: proposed`; ratification requires a separately approved Product Owner gate under the `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-NNN` family). `ADR-DRAFT-P03-004` is **still not ratified** (ADR draft remains `status: proposed`; ratification requires a separately approved Product Owner gate under the `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-NNN` family per `I-2`, and only after the underlying `R-4` recommendation is separately ratified). The revision makes `R-4` **eligible** for a later separate Product Owner recommendation ratification under `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-NNN`, if the Product Owner selects it; and makes `ADR-DRAFT-P03-004` **eligible** for a later separate Product Owner ADR ratification under `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-NNN` only after `R-4` is later ratified, preserving `I-2`.

  - Step E revision is the **prescribed remediation** in `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_RATIFICATION_PLAN.md` §6 for `R-4` / `ADR-DRAFT-P03-004`: "Needs an enumerated runtime-context-pack acceptance-criteria set (generator provenance, freshness check, staleness halt evidence, subordination clause, hard token cap, observable generation, reversibility, explicit non-elevation) before full ratification. ## DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-006

- decision_id: `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-006`
- status: `RATIFIED`
- decision: Ratify P03 architecture recommendation `R-4` (**Context Architecture**) from `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_EVALUATION_PACKAGE.md` §6, adopting **Option X-B** (lightweight runtime context pack) as the preferred future direction, conditional on a future separately approved generation gate (source-package **Gate G-6**) that demonstrably satisfies each of the eight explicit runtime-context-pack acceptance criteria added by the Step E revision under `DEC-P03-ARCH-REVISION-002`: **1. generator provenance**, **2. freshness check**, **3. staleness halt evidence**, **4. subordination clause**, **5. hard token cap**, **6. observable generation**, **7. reversibility**, **8. explicit non-elevation**. Until Gate G-6 is separately approved and satisfied, **Option X-A** (cold-start full canonical read) remains in effect as the currently-active canonical baseline. This ratification uses the Step E-revised package wording of §6 (`R-4`) **verbatim**. This decision is the **sixth row in the `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-NNN` family**, sequenced after `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-002`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-003`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-004`, and `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-005`. Option `X-B` generation is **not authorized by this ratification under any condition**; generation itself remains source-package Gate G-6, a separately approved future Product Owner gate. `ADR-DRAFT-P03-004` (Context Architecture Realization) is **not** canonicalized by this ratification; canonical ADR ratification under the `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-NNN` family per `I-2` (`DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-004`) is now **eligible** (the underlying `R-4` recommendation is ratified by this decision) and requires a separately approved Product Owner gate.
- ratified_by: `Rauf Alizada`
- ratified_at: `2026-06-28`
- source_task: `CONT-P03-ARCH-001`
- source_activation: `DEC-P03-ACTIVATION-001`
- drafted_by: `Claude Code`
- reviewed_by: `Product Owner`
- recommendation_ratified: `R-4` (Context Architecture) — Option `X-B` (lightweight runtime context pack) as preferred future direction, conditional on Gate G-6 and the eight explicit runtime-context-pack acceptance criteria, per the Step E-revised package wording ratified under `DEC-P03-ARCH-REVISION-002`; Option `X-A` (cold-start full read) remains the currently-active canonical baseline until Gate G-6.
- decision_family: `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-NNN` (per `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_RATIFICATION_PLAN.md` §9). This decision is the **sixth row** in the `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-NNN` family, sequenced after `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-002`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-003`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-004`, and `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-005`.
- related_prior_decisions: `DEC-P03-ARCH-REVISION-002`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-005`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-005`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-REVISION-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-004`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-004`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-003`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-003`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-002`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-002`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-004`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-003`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-002`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001`, `DEC-P03-ACTIVATION-001`.

- consistency_with_prior_recommendation_ratifications: Consistent with `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-001` (`R-5` / Option `B-B`), `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-002` (`R-1` / Option `D-B`), `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-003` (`R-3` / Option `C-C`), `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-004` (`R-6` / Option `A-C`), and `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-005` (`R-2` / staged `S-A` → `S-B` → (post-P04) `S-C`). The canonical-wins discipline already adopted is preserved here for the Context Architecture dimension as a **gated, not-immediate-generation** posture: Option `X-A` is the current canonical baseline; Option `X-B` remains a separately approved future gate (Gate G-6) and is not adopted as currently-active by this ratification. `R-1`, `R-2`, `R-3`, `R-5`, `R-6`, `ADR-DRAFT-P03-001`, `ADR-DRAFT-P03-002`, `ADR-DRAFT-P03-003`, `ADR-DRAFT-P03-005`, and `ADR-DRAFT-P03-006` remain canonical and are not re-ratified.
- safety_basis:
  - The recommendation **directly addresses** the `P03-blocking` source-register rows that the G-4 classification (`DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001`) records as conditioned by `R-4` / `ADR-DRAFT-P03-004` per `governance/P03_G4_CLASSIFICATION_PLAN.md`: `OQ-P02-D-005` (`Generated Context Pack` naming/scope/boundary — §5 line 101), `OQ-P02-C-004` (Context-Bound integration into ratified context-policy set — §5 line 118), `P02-RISK-003` (Generated Context Treated as Canonical — §6 line 132), `P02-RISK-004` (Stale Generated Context — §6 line 133), and `P02-ROAD-006` (Decide Generated-Context Pack Naming, Scope, Freshness, Trust Boundary — §7 line 159). Ratifying `R-4` under `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-006` architecture-posture-**bounds** these rows at the canonical realization surface (Option `X-A` interim baseline; Option `X-B` gated by Gate G-6 and the eight explicit acceptance criteria) without mutating those rows in `governance/OPEN_QUESTIONS.md` or `governance/RISK_REGISTER.md`.
  - Structural cross-cutting `P03-blocking` risks `P02-RISK-001` (Product Owner Authority Confusion / Invalid Identity), `P02-RISK-002` (Active-Task Invariant Violation), `P02-RISK-005` (Unauthorized Commit/Push or Approval-Verb Violation), `P02-RISK-006` (Destructive Git Command Without Explicit Approval), and `P02-RISK-018` (P02 Open Questions Remaining Unresolved) are reaffirmed without mutation by this ratification.
  - The gated-not-immediate-generation posture preserves ratified `governance/CONTEXT_POLICY.md` canonical-wins discipline (P-4), ratified `governance/CONTEXT_BUDGET.md` token-cap discipline, ratified `governance/CONTEXT_RETRIEVAL_PROTOCOL.md` retrieval-mode discipline, and ratified `governance/NEVER_AUTOMATIC.md` never-automatic surface (P-9).
  - `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-006` satisfies `I-1` (per `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-001`): it is recorded as its own distinct row in `governance/DECISION_LOG.md`, separate from any other decision row, and is the sixth row in its decision-id family.
  - `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-006` satisfies `I-7` (per `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-002`): the `non_authorizations:` section below explicitly enumerates what this decision does not authorize, including explicit non-authorization of runtime context pack generation under any condition.
  - `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-006` preserves `I-8` (per `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-003`): it does not open P03 closeout and does not open P04 GO; both require separately approved Product Owner gates.
  - `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-006` preserves `I-2` (per `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-004`): it does not canonicalize `ADR-DRAFT-P03-004`; canonical ADR canonicalization for `ADR-DRAFT-P03-004` under the `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-NNN` family is now **eligible** because the underlying `R-4` recommendation is ratified by this decision, and remains a separately approved Product Owner gate.
- source_register_dependency_surface: `R-4` ratification under `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-006` architecture-posture-**bounds** the following `P03-blocking` source-register rows under `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001` (per `governance/P03_G4_CLASSIFICATION_PLAN.md`): `OQ-P02-D-005`, `OQ-P02-C-004`, `P02-RISK-003`, `P02-RISK-004`, and `P02-ROAD-006`. No source-register row is mutated by this decision. Final per-row disposition / acceptance / mitigation / transfer / scheduling for each of these rows remains a separately approved Product Owner gate.
- forward_application:
  - The canonical Context Architecture posture for v1 is: Option `X-A` (cold-start full canonical read) is the currently-active canonical baseline. Option `X-B` (lightweight runtime context pack) becomes eligible only under a separately approved Product Owner Gate G-6 that demonstrably satisfies all eight explicit runtime-context-pack acceptance criteria; this ratification does **not** authorize Gate G-6 or any runtime context pack generation.
  - `ADR-DRAFT-P03-004` (Context Architecture Realization) canonicalization under the `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-NNN` family per `I-2` (`DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-004`) is now **eligible** because the underlying `R-4` recommendation is ratified by this decision; canonicalization requires a separately approved Product Owner gate.
  - Any future revision affecting `R-4` requires a successor `DEC-P03-ARCH-REVISION-NNN` decision (numbering monotonic, starting from `003`) and/or a successor `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-NNN` decision that explicitly supersedes `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-006`.
  - The ratification does not pre-authorize any later step: Gate G-6 (runtime context pack generation), Gate G-7 (P03 closeout), Gate G-8 (P04 GO), or any future `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-NNN` ADR canonicalization for `ADR-DRAFT-P03-004` each requires its own separately approved Product Owner gate per `governance/CHANGE_PROTOCOL.md`.

  - Does **not** modify `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_EVALUATION_PACKAGE.md` or elevate its overall status. The package remains `PROPOSED_INACTIVE` / `NOT_RATIFIED`; the Step E-revised `R-4` wording remains the canonical text of the proposed `R-4` material in the package; what is now ratified as canonical architecture posture is the `R-4` recommendation row in `governance/DECISION_LOG.md` under `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-006`.
  - Does **not** modify `governance/P02_DOMAIN_DISCOVERY_DRAFT.md`, `governance/P02_SECURITY_TRUST_REQUIREMENTS_DRAFT.md`, `governance/P02_DATA_CLASSIFICATION_SENSITIVE_BOUNDARY_DRAFT.md`, the ratified context-policy set (`governance/CONTEXT_POLICY.md`, `governance/CONTEXT_BUDGET.md`, `governance/CONTEXT_RETRIEVAL_PROTOCOL.md`), `governance/TRUST_BOUNDARIES.md`, `governance/NEVER_AUTOMATIC.md`, or any other ratified P02 artifact.
  - Does **not** mutate `governance/OPEN_QUESTIONS.md`, `governance/RISK_REGISTER.md`, or `governance/ROADMAP.md`. `OQ-P02-D-005`, `OQ-P02-C-004`, `P02-RISK-003`, `P02-RISK-004`, and `P02-ROAD-006` remain in their existing source-register states; no row is resolved, accepted, disposed, mitigated, transferred, scheduled, or transitioned.

  - Does **not** accept, dispose, mitigate, transfer, or otherwise transition any `P02-RISK-*` row in the source register. `P02-RISK-003` and `P02-RISK-004` are bounded by this ratification for the canonical architecture posture only; final risk disposition remains a separately approved Product Owner gate.

  - Does **not** authorize implementation, project code, dependency installation, lockfile or manifest changes, or license selection.
  - Does **not** authorize creation, generation, or population of any adapter-contract file, classification-registry file, adapter implementation, connector code, or security enforcement control.
  - Does **not** authorize P04/P05 activation; does not create any P04 or P05 task; does not open P03 closeout (source-package Gate G-7); does not open P04 GO (source-package Gate G-8).
  - Does **not** create or modify `governance/PRODUCT_OWNER.md` (absent and remains absent).

  - `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-002`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-003`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-004`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-002`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-002`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-003`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-003`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-004`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-004`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-REVISION-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-005`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-005`, and `DEC-P03-ARCH-REVISION-002` remain canonical and unsuperseded.

## DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-006

- decision_id: `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-006`
- status: `RATIFIED`
- decision: Canonicalize `ADR-DRAFT-P03-004` (**Context Architecture Realization**) verbatim from `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_EVALUATION_PACKAGE.md` §7 as Step E-revised under `DEC-P03-ARCH-REVISION-002` — adopt **Option X-B** (lightweight runtime context pack) as preferred future direction, conditional on a separately approved future generation gate (source-package **Gate G-6**) that demonstrably satisfies each of the eight explicit runtime-context-pack acceptance criteria: **1. generator provenance**, **2. freshness check**, **3. staleness halt evidence**, **4. subordination clause**, **5. hard token cap**, **6. observable generation**, **7. reversibility**, **8. explicit non-elevation**. Until Gate G-6 is separately approved and satisfied, **Option X-A** (cold-start full canonical read) remains in effect as the currently-active canonical baseline. This decision is the **sixth row in the `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-NNN` family**, sequenced after `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-002`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-003`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-004`, and `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-005`. This canonicalization is eligible per `I-2` (`DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-004`) because the underlying `R-4` recommendation is already ratified under `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-006`. Option `X-B` generation remains **not authorized by this ratification under any condition**; generation itself remains source-package Gate G-6, a separately approved future Product Owner gate.
- ratified_by: `Rauf Alizada`
- ratified_at: `2026-06-28`
- source_task: `CONT-P03-ARCH-001`
- source_activation: `DEC-P03-ACTIVATION-001`
- drafted_by: `Claude Code`
- reviewed_by: `Product Owner`
- adr_ratified: `ADR-DRAFT-P03-004` (Context Architecture Realization) — Option `X-B` (lightweight runtime context pack) as preferred future direction, conditional on Gate G-6 and the eight explicit runtime-context-pack acceptance criteria; Option `X-A` (cold-start full read) remains the currently-active canonical baseline until Gate G-6.
- decision_family: `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-NNN` (per `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_RATIFICATION_PLAN.md` §9). This decision is the **sixth row** in the `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-NNN` family, sequenced after `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-002`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-003`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-004`, and `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-005`.
- related_prior_decisions: `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-006`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-REVISION-002`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-005`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-005`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-REVISION-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-004`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-004`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-003`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-003`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-002`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-002`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-004`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-003`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-002`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001`, `DEC-P03-ACTIVATION-001`.

The package itself remains `PROPOSED_INACTIVE` / `NOT_RATIFIED`; what is now canonical Context Architecture Realization ADR is the `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-006` row in `governance/DECISION_LOG.md`.
