The gated, not-immediate-generation posture is preserved here at the ADR level for the Context Architecture dimension: Option `X-A` is the current canonical baseline; Option `X-B` remains a separately approved future gate (Gate G-6) and is not adopted as currently-active by this ratification. `ADR-DRAFT-P03-001`, `ADR-DRAFT-P03-002`, `ADR-DRAFT-P03-003`, `ADR-DRAFT-P03-005`, and `ADR-DRAFT-P03-006` remain canonical and are not re-ratified.
- safety_basis:
  - Canonicalizing `ADR-DRAFT-P03-004` at the ADR level **reinforces** the architecture-posture bound already established by `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-006` on the `P03-blocking` source-register rows `OQ-P02-D-005` (`Generated Context Pack` naming/scope/boundary — `governance/P03_G4_CLASSIFICATION_PLAN.md` §5 line 101), `OQ-P02-C-004` (Context-Bound integration into ratified context-policy set — §5 line 118), `P02-RISK-003` (Generated Context Treated as Canonical — §6 line 132), `P02-RISK-004` (Stale Generated Context — §6 line 133), and `P02-ROAD-006` (Decide Generated-Context Pack Naming, Scope, Freshness, Trust Boundary — §7 line 159), without mutating those rows in `governance/OPEN_QUESTIONS.md` or `governance/RISK_REGISTER.md`.
  - Structural cross-cutting `P03-blocking` risks `P02-RISK-001` (Product Owner Authority Confusion / Invalid Identity), `P02-RISK-002` (Active-Task Invariant Violation), `P02-RISK-005` (Unauthorized Commit/Push or Approval-Verb Violation), `P02-RISK-006` (Destructive Git Command Without Explicit Approval), and `P02-RISK-018` (P02 Open Questions Remaining Unresolved) are reaffirmed without mutation by this ratification.
  - The gated-not-immediate-generation posture preserves ratified `governance/CONTEXT_POLICY.md` canonical-wins discipline (P-4), ratified `governance/CONTEXT_BUDGET.md` token-cap discipline, ratified `governance/CONTEXT_RETRIEVAL_PROTOCOL.md` retrieval-mode discipline, and ratified `governance/NEVER_AUTOMATIC.md` never-automatic surface (P-9).
  - `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-006` satisfies `I-1` (per `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-001`): unique row in the `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-NNN` family, sixth row.
  - `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-006` satisfies `I-2` (per `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-004`): `ADR-DRAFT-P03-004` is canonicalized only because the underlying `R-4` recommendation is already ratified under `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-006`.

No source-register row is mutated by this decision. Final per-row disposition remains a separately approved Product Owner gate.

- predecessor_decisions: `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-006`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-REVISION-002`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-005`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-005`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-REVISION-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-004`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-004`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-003`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-003`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-002`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-002`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-004`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-003`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-002`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001`, `DEC-P03-ACTIVATION-001`.

Does **not** re-ratify `R-4` (remains ratified under `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-006`). Does **not** re-ratify or modify any other ADR or recommendation. Does **not** ratify any criterion (`I-3`, `I-4`, `I-5`, `I-6`). ## DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-005

- decision_id: `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-005`
- status: `RATIFIED`
- decision: Ratify P03 implementation-readiness criterion `I-3` from `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_EVALUATION_PACKAGE.md` §8 as canonical procedural discipline under `CONT-P03-ARCH-001`. Ratified criterion text: "any `OQ-P02-*` open question that the Product Owner classifies as P04-blocking has been resolved through a separately approved Product Owner ratification before P04 GO; classification itself is a separate Product Owner-approved diff and is **not** performed by this package." Classification has since been separately performed and ratified under `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001` (28 `OQ-P02-*` rows classified; 14 rows across all three source registers classified `P04-blocking`). Ratifying `I-3` codifies the binding rule that every `OQ-P02-*` row classified `P04-blocking` under `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001` must be resolved through its own separately approved Product Owner ratification before P04 GO (source-package Gate G-8); ratifying `I-3` does not itself resolve any such row.
- ratified_by: `Rauf Alizada`
- ratified_at: `2026-06-28`
- source_task: `CONT-P03-ARCH-001`
- source_activation: `DEC-P03-ACTIVATION-001`
- drafted_by: `Claude Code`
- reviewed_by: `Product Owner`
- criterion_ratified: `I-3` (`governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_EVALUATION_PACKAGE.md` §8).
- decision_family: `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-NNN` (per `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_RATIFICATION_PLAN.md` §9). This decision is the fifth row in the `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-NNN` family, sequenced after `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-001` (`I-1`), `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-002` (`I-7`), `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-003` (`I-8`), and `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-004` (`I-2`).
- related_prior_decisions: `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-006`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-006`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-004`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-003`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-002`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001`, `DEC-P03-ACTIVATION-001`.
- safety_basis:
  - `I-3` was previously blocked on G-4 classification (Step B); that dependency is now satisfied because `governance/P03_G4_CLASSIFICATION_PLAN.md` is `Ratified / RATIFIED` under `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001`, which classified all 28 `OQ-P02-*` rows (27 `P03-blocking`, 14 `P04-blocking`, 21 `deferred-with-acceptance` across all three registers combined).
  - `I-3` is a procedural / phase-boundary discipline rule binding future per-row resolution gates for `OQ-P02-*` rows classified `P04-blocking`. It does not itself resolve, accept, dispose, or otherwise transition any `OQ-P02-*` row.
  - `I-3` does not require modifying `governance/OPEN_QUESTIONS.md`, `governance/RISK_REGISTER.md`, or `governance/ROADMAP.md`.
  - `I-3` does not require revising `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_EVALUATION_PACKAGE.md` or `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_RATIFICATION_PLAN.md`; both remain `PROPOSED_INACTIVE` / `NOT_RATIFIED` as canonical reference framing only.
  - `I-3` does not require modifying or reclassifying any row of `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001`.
  - `I-3` is complementary to `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-001` (`I-1`), `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-002` (`I-7`), `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-003` (`I-8`), and `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-004` (`I-2`) and does not conflict with any of them; the five procedural rules co-bind every future P03 ratification gate and every future P04-GO gate.
- forward_application:
  - Every `OQ-P02-*` row classified `P04-blocking` under `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001` must be resolved through its own separately approved Product Owner ratification before P04 GO (source-package Gate G-8); a bundled or implicit resolution across multiple rows is not permitted absent an explicit Product Owner decision stating otherwise.
  - Resolution rows are recorded in `governance/DECISION_LOG.md` and co-apply with `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-001` (row-uniqueness) and `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-002` (explicit non-authorization disclosure).
  - This forward-application clause restates and binds `I-3`; it does not itself resolve any `OQ-P02-*` row or open P04 GO.

  - `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-001..004` and `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-006` are canonical at HEAD `5d4e03031bb5b987671f7252414a765b169aad29`.

  - `I-5` does not require modifying or reclassifying any row of `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001`.

- forward_application:
  - Every `P02-ROAD-*` roadmap item classified `P04-blocking` under `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001`, and any other `P02-ROAD-*` item required by a ratified architecture decision, must be scheduled under its own separately approved Product Owner gate before P04 GO (source-package Gate G-8); a bundled or implicit scheduling across multiple items is not permitted absent an explicit Product Owner decision stating otherwise.

## DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-008

- decision_id: `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-008`
- status: `RATIFIED`
- decision: Ratify P03 implementation-readiness criterion `I-6` from `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_EVALUATION_PACKAGE.md` §8 as canonical procedural discipline under `CONT-P03-ARCH-001`. Ratified criterion text: "ratified architecture decisions explicitly preserve canonical-wins (canonical governance over derived/generated context), the active-task invariant, Product Owner identity encoding (`Rauf Alizada` only), and the never-automatic surface." Unlike `I-3`/`I-4`/`I-5`, `I-6` carries no G-4 classification dependency; it is ratified here standalone, as a standing procedural discipline binding the form of every ratified architecture decision, rather than embedded into another decision row as non-bindingly recommended by `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_RATIFICATION_PLAN.md` §6.

This decision is the eighth row in the `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-NNN` family, sequenced after `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-001` (`I-1`), `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-002` (`I-7`), `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-003` (`I-8`), `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-004` (`I-2`), `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-005` (`I-3`), `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-006` (`I-4`), and `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-007` (`I-5`).

- safety_basis:
  - `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_RATIFICATION_PLAN.md` §6 (echoed at §5 and §9) lists `I-6` under "Items Requiring Revision Before Ratification" with a non-binding recommendation that `I-6` substance be linked into every ratified architecture decision row rather than ratified as a standalone procedural row. That recommendation is advisory only: the plan remains `PROPOSED_INACTIVE` / `NOT_RATIFIED`, and its recommended ratification sequence is explicitly "proposed only" — the Product Owner may reorder, skip, or reject any step. The Product Owner has elected standalone `I-6` ratification; this decision records that election. The plan's embed-only recommendation is not itself ratified or adopted.
  - `I-6` carries no G-4 classification dependency, unlike `I-3` (`DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-005`), `I-4` (`DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-006`), and `I-5` (`DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-007`), each of which required `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001` to classify `OQ-P02-*` / `P02-RISK-*` / `P02-ROAD-*` rows before ratification. `I-6` binds the form of every ratified architecture decision directly and required no such prerequisite.
  - Every architecture decision already ratified in this project (`DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-001..006`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-001..006`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-REVISION-001..002`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-001..007`) already restates canonical-wins, the active-task invariant, Product Owner identity encoding, and/or explicit non-authorization language in its own fields; ratifying `I-6` makes that existing practice an explicit, binding, forward-looking rule.

- forward_application:
  - Every architecture decision ratified after this decision under the `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-NNN`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-NNN`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-NNN`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-NNN`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-REVISION-NNN`, and `DEC-P03-CLOSEOUT-NNN` families must explicitly preserve canonical-wins, the active-task invariant, Product Owner identity encoding (`Rauf Alizada` only), and the never-automatic surface, either by restating the substance or by named reference to this decision.

## DEC-P03-ARCH-DISP-001

- decision_id: `DEC-P03-ARCH-DISP-001`
- status: `RATIFIED`
- decision: Ratify the Context-cluster disposition of five `P03-blocking` source-register rows classified under `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001` — `OQ-P02-D-005`, `OQ-P02-C-004`, `P02-RISK-003`, `P02-RISK-004`, and `P02-ROAD-006` — on the basis of the already-ratified Context Architecture posture (`R-4` ratified under `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-006`; `ADR-DRAFT-P03-004` canonicalized under `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-006`, both carrying verbatim the Step E-revised eight-item runtime-context-pack acceptance-criteria set ratified under `DEC-P03-ARCH-REVISION-002`: generator provenance, freshness check, staleness halt evidence, subordination clause, hard token cap, observable generation, reversibility, explicit non-elevation). This is the first row in a new `DEC-P03-ARCH-DISP-NNN` decision family, introduced by explicit Product Owner instruction to record per-row `P03-blocking` disposition outcomes distinctly from recommendation (`DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-NNN`), ADR (`DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-NNN`), criterion (`DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-NNN`), classification (`DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-NNN`), and revision (`DEC-P03-ARCH-REVISION-NNN`) decisions, consistent with the `DEC-P03-CLOSEOUT-NNN`-adjacent family pattern anticipated by `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_RATIFICATION_PLAN.md` §9.
- ratified_by: `Rauf Alizada`
- ratified_at: `2026-07-01`
- source_task: `CONT-P03-ARCH-001`
- source_activation: `DEC-P03-ACTIVATION-001`
- drafted_by: `Claude Code`
- reviewed_by: `Product Owner`
- rows_dispositioned:
  - `OQ-P02-D-005` (Runtime Context Assembly; conditions `R-4` acceptance criteria) — **disposition: resolved**. The architecture-level question of how runtime context is assembled is answered end-to-end by `R-4` / `ADR-DRAFT-P03-004`: Option `X-A` (cold-start full canonical read) is the current canonical baseline; Option `X-B` (lightweight runtime context pack) remains conditional on a separately approved future Gate G-6 satisfying the eight explicit acceptance criteria. Resolution is at the architecture-decision level only; it does not authorize, generate, or schedule any runtime context pack.
  - `OQ-P02-C-004` (Context freshness/staleness detection; conditions `R-4` subordination clause) — **disposition: resolved**. The freshness-check and staleness-halt-evidence criteria (two of the eight explicit acceptance criteria ratified under `DEC-P03-ARCH-REVISION-002` and canonicalized under `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-006`) directly answer the freshness/staleness-detection architecture question: no freshness/staleness detection mechanism may exist because no Option `X-B` runtime context pack is authorized until Gate G-6 demonstrates satisfaction of those criteria.
  - `P02-RISK-003` (Stale or Drifted Runtime Context; `R-4` subordination/non-elevation criterion) — **disposition: disposed (mitigated, architecture-level)**. The freshness-check, staleness-halt-evidence, subordination-clause, and explicit-non-elevation criteria mitigate this risk at the architecture level by making them mandatory preconditions of any future Gate G-6; until Gate G-6 is separately approved and satisfied, Option `X-A` (full canonical read, no drift surface) remains the enforced baseline. Full operational mitigation remains pending the future Gate G-6.
  - `P02-RISK-004` (Context Budget / Token Overrun; `R-4` freshness/staleness criterion) — **disposition: disposed (mitigated, architecture-level)**. The hard-token-cap criterion (one of the eight explicit acceptance criteria) mitigates this risk at the architecture level by making token-cap enforcement a mandatory precondition of any future Gate G-6. Full operational mitigation remains pending the future Gate G-6.
  - `P02-ROAD-006` (Runtime Context Pack milestone; drives `R-4` acceptance criteria) — **disposition: resolved (architecture-decision level)**. The architecture decision underlying this roadmap item is fully ratified end-to-end (`R-4` under `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-006`; `ADR-DRAFT-P03-004` under `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-006`). Per `I-5` (ratified under `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-007`), actual scheduling of this roadmap item's execution remains a separately approved future Product Owner gate; this disposition resolves only the item's `P03-blocking` architecture-decision dependency and does not schedule execution.
- decision_family: `DEC-P03-ARCH-DISP-NNN` (new family, per `governance/P03_ARCHITECTURE_RATIFICATION_PLAN.md` §9 decision-id-family pattern). This is the first row in the family.
- related_prior_decisions: `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-008`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-007`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-006`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-005`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-006`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-006`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-REVISION-002`, `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001`, `DEC-P03-ACTIVATION-001`.
- safety_basis:
  - All five rows were classified `P03-blocking` under `DEC-P03-ARCH-CLASS-001` and were each already architecture-bounded end-to-end by `DEC-P03-ARCH-RECO-006` (`R-4` ratification) and reinforced at the ADR level by `DEC-P03-ARCH-ADR-006` (`ADR-DRAFT-P03-004` canonicalization), both carrying the Step E-revised eight-item acceptance-criteria set ratified under `DEC-P03-ARCH-REVISION-002`.
  - Disposition here is a bookkeeping act that records the outcome already established by prior ratifications; it does not perform new tradeoff analysis, does not reopen the Context Architecture evaluation, and does not add, remove, or reweight any acceptance criterion.
  - The two risk dispositions (`P02-RISK-003`, `P02-RISK-004`) are recorded as "mitigated, architecture-level" rather than "fully mitigated" because operational proof of mitigation (i.e., a Gate G-6 satisfying the eight criteria) has not occurred; this distinction preserves accuracy and does not overstate the disposition.
  - The roadmap disposition (`P02-ROAD-006`) is recorded as "resolved (architecture-decision level)" rather than "scheduled" because scheduling remains a separate act under `I-5` (`DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-007`); this decision does not schedule the item.
  - This disposition is consistent with ratified `governance/CONTEXT_POLICY.md` canonical-wins discipline (P-4) and ratified `governance/NEVER_AUTOMATIC.md` never-automatic surface (P-9), and preserves the four `I-6` elements (canonical-wins, active-task invariant, Product Owner identity encoding, never-automatic surface) per `DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-008`.
- forward_application:
  - `OQ-P02-D-005` and `OQ-P02-C-004` are recorded as resolved and require no further Product Owner action to satisfy their `P03-blocking` status; they remain visible in `governance/OPEN_QUESTIONS.md` unchanged in content, with this decision serving as the disposition record of record.
  - `P02-RISK-003` and `P02-RISK-004` are recorded as disposed (mitigated, architecture-level) and satisfy `I-4`'s `P03-blocking` counterpart discipline for these two rows; full operational mitigation evidence remains a future Gate G-6 concern and does not need to be re-litigated at P03 closeout.
  - `P02-ROAD-006` is recorded as resolved at the architecture-decision level; its eventual execution scheduling remains subject to `I-5` (`DEC-P03-ARCH-CRIT-007`) and a separately approved future Product Owner gate.
  - This forward-application clause records the disposition outcome for these five rows only; it does not itself dispose, resolve, or schedule any other `OQ-P02-*`, `P02-RISK-*`, or `P02-ROAD-*` row.
